import os, re, math, pandas as pd, xml.etree.ElementTree as ET
from pathlib import Path

[ASSISTANT]
code = r'''import re
import math
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox, ttk
from html.parser import HTMLParser
import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET

import pandas as pd


# ----------------------------
# Helpers
# ----------------------------

def canon(s: str) -> str:
    """Lowercase + remove non-alnum for robust column matching."""
    return re.sub(r'[^a-z0-9]+', '', (s or '').strip().lower())


def normalize_bin(bin_name: str):
    """
    Dynamic bin parser:
      '2A33' -> row='A',  num=33,  norm='A33'
      'AA07' -> row='AA', num=7,   norm='AA07'
      'R1'   -> row='R',  num=1,   norm='R01'

    Returns (row_id, bin_num, normalized_bin_string).
    If it doesn't match letters+digits, returns (None, None, original).
    """
    s = str(bin_name).strip()
    m = re.match(r'^(\d+)?([A-Za-z]+)(\d+)$', s)
    if not m:
        return None, None, s
    row_id = m.group(2).upper()
    num = int(m.group(3))
    return row_id, num, f"{row_id}{num:02d}"


def to_num(x, default=0.0):
    try:
        if x is None:
            return default
        if isinstance(x, float) and (math.isnan(x) or math.isinf(x)):
            return default
        s = str(x).strip()
        if s == '':
            return default
        return float(s.replace(',', ''))
    except Exception:
        return default


# ----------------------------
# HTML table parser (no external deps)
# ----------------------------

class _SAPHTMLTableParser(HTMLParser):
    """
    Minimal parser for SAP 'Report output' HTML exports:
    - finds the first <table> and extracts rows/cells text
    """
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.in_table = False
        self.in_tr = False
        self.in_td = False
        self.tables = []
        self._rows = []
        self._row = []
        self._cell = []

    def handle_starttag(self, tag, attrs):
        tag = tag.lower()
        if tag == 'table':
            # SAP uses class="list", but we accept any first table
            self.in_table = True
            self._rows = []
        elif self.in_table and tag == 'tr':
            self.in_tr = True
            self._row = []
        elif self.in_table and self.in_tr and tag in ('td', 'th'):
            self.in_td = True
            self._cell = []
        # ignore everything else

    def handle_endtag(self, tag):
        tag = tag.lower()
        if tag == 'table' and self.in_table:
            self.in_table = False
            if self._rows:
                self.tables.append(self._rows)
            self._rows = []
        elif tag == 'tr' and self.in_tr:
            self.in_tr = False
            if self._row:
                self._rows.append(self._row)
            self._row = []
        elif tag in ('td', 'th') and self.in_td:
            self.in_td = False
            cell_text = ''.join(self._cell)
            # normalize whitespace / nbsp
            cell_text = cell_text.replace('\xa0', ' ')
            cell_text = re.sub(r'\s+', ' ', cell_text).strip()
            self._row.append(cell_text)
            self._cell = []

    def handle_data(self, data):
        if self.in_table and self.in_tr and self.in_td and data:
            self._cell.append(data)


def parse_sap_html(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8', errors='replace') as f:
        html = f.read()
    p = _SAPHTMLTableParser()
    p.feed(html)
    if not p.tables:
        return pd.DataFrame()
    # pick the table that contains StorageBin header if available
    best = p.tables[0]
    for t in p.tables:
        joined = ' '.join(' '.join(r) for r in t[:3]).lower()
        if 'storagebin' in joined or 'storage bin' in joined:
            best = t
            break
    # first row is headers
    headers = best[0]
    data_rows = best[1:]
    # pad rows to header length
    fixed = []
    for r in data_rows:
        if len(r) < len(headers):
            r = r + [''] * (len(headers) - len(r))
        fixed.append(r[:len(headers)])
    return pd.DataFrame(fixed, columns=headers)


# ----------------------------
# XML parsers
# ----------------------------

def parse_inventoryexport_xml(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    """
    Parses custom XML like:
      <InventoryExport><Record><Storage_Bin>...</Storage_Bin> ... </Record>...</InventoryExport>
    """
    tree = ET.parse(path)
    root = tree.getroot()
    if canon(root.tag) not in ('inventoryexport',):
        # still might be this format even if wrapped; detect Record children
        recs = root.findall('.//Record')
        if not recs:
            return pd.DataFrame()
    else:
        recs = root.findall('.//Record')

    rows = []
    for rec in recs:
        # tag names vary with underscores/spaces
        d = {canon(child.tag): (child.text or '').strip() for child in rec}
        rows.append(d)
    if not rows:
        return pd.DataFrame()
    return pd.DataFrame(rows)


def parse_spreadsheetml_grid_xml(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    """
    Parses Excel 2003 SpreadsheetML where data is in Worksheet/Table/Row/Cell/Data.
    """
    tree = ET.parse(path)
    root = tree.getroot()

    ns = {'ss': 'urn:schemas-microsoft-com:office:spreadsheet'}
    # If no worksheet, bail
    ws = root.find('.//ss:Worksheet', ns)
    if ws is None:
        return pd.DataFrame()

    table = ws.find('.//ss:Table', ns)
    if table is None:
        return pd.DataFrame()

    rows = []
    for row in table.findall('ss:Row', ns):
        cells = []
        col_idx = 1
        for cell in row.findall('ss:Cell', ns):
            idx_attr = cell.get('{urn:schemas-microsoft-com:office:spreadsheet}Index')
            if idx_attr:
                try:
                    col_idx = int(idx_attr)
                except Exception:
                    pass
            # ensure list size
            while len(cells) < col_idx - 1:
                cells.append('')
            data = cell.find('ss:Data', ns)
            cells.append((data.text or '').strip() if data is not None else '')
            col_idx += 1
        # keep non-empty rows
        if any(cells):
            rows.append(cells)

    if not rows:
        return pd.DataFrame()

    # header is first row
    header = rows[0]
    data_rows = rows[1:]
    max_len = max(len(r) for r in rows)
    header = (header + [''] * (max_len - len(header)))[:max_len]
    fixed = []
    for r in data_rows:
        r = (r + [''] * (max_len - len(r)))[:max_len]
        fixed.append(r)

    return pd.DataFrame(fixed, columns=header)


def parse_spreadsheetml_piped_xml(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    """
    Parses SpreadsheetML where each row is a pipe-delimited line stored in ss:Data.
    """
    tree = ET.parse(path)
    root = tree.getroot()
    ns = {'ss': 'urn:schemas-microsoft-com:office:spreadsheet'}

    lines = []
    for data_node in root.findall('.//ss:Data', ns):
        t = data_node.text or ''
        if '|' not in t:
            continue
        for line in t.splitlines():
            line = line.strip()
            if line.startswith('|'):
                lines.append(line)

    if not lines:
        return pd.DataFrame()

    # find header line
    header_line = None
    for l in lines[:50]:
        if 'storagebin' in l.lower():
            header_line = l
            break
    if header_line is None:
        header_line = lines[0]

    def split_line(l):
        parts = [p.strip() for p in l.split('|')]
        # drop leading/trailing empties typical in SAP exports
        if parts and parts[0] == '':
            parts = parts[1:]
        if parts and parts[-1] == '':
            parts = parts[:-1]
        return parts

    header = split_line(header_line)
    data_lines = [l for l in lines if l != header_line and '---' not in l]

    fixed = []
    for l in data_lines:
        parts = split_line(l)
        if len(parts) < len(header):
            parts = parts + [''] * (len(header) - len(parts))
        fixed.append(parts[:len(header)])

    return pd.DataFrame(fixed, columns=header)


def parse_xml_auto(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    """
    Auto-detect supported XML formats:
    - custom InventoryExport/Record XML
    - SpreadsheetML piped
    - SpreadsheetML grid
    """
    # First try simple custom record XML quickly by peeking the start
    with open(path, 'rb') as f:
        head = f.read(4096).decode('utf-8', errors='replace').lower()

    if '<inventoryexport' in head or '<record' in head:
        df = parse_inventoryexport_xml(path)
        if not df.empty:
            return df

    # SpreadsheetML?
    if 'urn:schemas-microsoft-com:office:spreadsheet' in head or '<workbook' in head:
        df = parse_spreadsheetml_piped_xml(path)
        if not df.empty:
            return df
        df = parse_spreadsheetml_grid_xml(path)
        if not df.empty:
            return df

    # fallback: try record XML anyway
    df = parse_inventoryexport_xml(path)
    return df


# ----------------------------
# Standardize columns
# ----------------------------

def standardize_snapshot_df(df: pd.DataFrame):
    """
    Convert any input DataFrame into standard columns:
      BinRaw, Material, Description, Qty, Capacity

    Uses fuzzy column matching.
    """
    if df is None or df.empty:
        return pd.DataFrame(), "No data found"

    cols = list(df.columns)

    # If the data frame came from InventoryExport XML, columns might already be canonicalized (no spaces).
    canon_map = {c: canon(str(c)) for c in cols}

    # candidates
    bin_keys = {'storagebin', 'storagebin', 'storagebin', 'storagebin', 'storagebin', 'storagebin', 'storagebin'}  # placeholder
    # We'll match by contains rather than exact sets.
    def find_col(*needles):
        for c in cols:
            cc = canon_map[c]
            for n in needles:
                if n in cc:
                    return c
        return None

    col_bin = find_col('storagebin', 'storagebin', 'storagebin', 'storagebin', 'storagebin', 'storagebin', 'storagebin') or \
              find_col('storagebin', 'storagebin') or \
              find_col('storagebin') or \
              find_col('storagebin') or \
              find_col('storagebin') or \
              find_col('storagebin') or \
              find_col('storagebin')
    # The above is silly but safe; we'll do real:
    col_bin = find_col('storagebin', 'storagebin') or find_col('storagebin') or find_col('storagebin')
    # Actually handle variations:
    if col_bin is None:
        col_bin = find_col('storagebin', 'storagebin')  # no-op

    # Better: explicit
    col_bin = find_col('storagebin') or find_col('storagebin') or find_col('storagebin')
    # We'll redo properly:
    col_bin = None
    for c in cols:
        cc = canon_map[c]
        if 'storagebin' in cc or (cc.endswith('bin') and 'storage' in cc) or cc == 'bin':
            col_bin = c
            break

    col_mat = None
    for c in cols:
        cc = canon_map[c]
        if cc in ('material', 'materia', 'product') or ('material' in cc and 'description' not in cc):
            col_mat = c
            break

    col_desc = None
    for c in cols:
        cc = canon_map[c]
        if 'materialdescription' in cc or cc == 'description' or 'matdesc' in cc:
            col_desc = c
            break

    # Prefer Total Stock over Available stock
    col_stock = None
    for c in cols:
        cc = canon_map[c]
        if 'totalstock' in cc or (cc == 'stock' and 'total' in head if False else False):
            col_stock = c
            break
    if col_stock is None:
        for c in cols:
            cc = canon_map[c]
            if 'availablestock' in cc or 'availstock' in cc or cc in ('qty', 'quantity', 'stock'):
                col_stock = c
                break

    col_cap = None
    for c in cols:
        cc = canon_map[c]
        if 'totalcapacity' in cc or (cc == 'capacity') or ('capacity' in cc and 'remaining' not in cc):
            col_cap = c
            break

    col_rem = None
    for c in cols:
        cc = canon_map[c]
        if 'remainingcapacity' in cc or ('remain' in cc and 'cap' in cc):
            col_rem = c
            break

    if col_bin is None or col_mat is None or col_stock is None:
        return pd.DataFrame(), f"Missing required columns. Found: {cols}"

    out = pd.DataFrame()
    out['BinRaw'] = df[col_bin].astype(str).str.strip()
    out['Material'] = df[col_mat].astype(str).str.strip()
    out['Description'] = df[col_desc].astype(str).str.strip() if col_desc is not None else ''
    out['Qty'] = df[col_stock].apply(to_num)
    out['Capacity'] = df[col_cap].apply(to_num) if col_cap is not None else 0.0
    remaining = df[col_rem].apply(to_num) if col_rem is not None else None

    # fill capacity if missing but remaining exists
    if (out['Capacity'] == 0).all() and remaining is not None and remaining.notna().any():
        out['Capacity'] = out['Qty'] + remaining

    # If capacity still 0, set to qty (prevents moving into unknown capacity bins)
    out['Capacity'] = out.apply(lambda r: r['Capacity'] if r['Capacity'] > 0 else r['Qty'], axis=1)

    # Drop empty materials
    out = out[out['Material'].astype(str).str.strip().ne('')].copy()
    out = out[~out['Material'].str.contains('empty', case=False, na=False)].copy()

    # Bin normalization
    norm = out['BinRaw'].apply(normalize_bin)
    out['Row'] = norm.apply(lambda x: x[0])
    out['BinNum'] = norm.apply(lambda x: x[1])
    out['Bin'] = norm.apply(lambda x: x[2])
    out = out[out['BinNum'].notna()].copy()
    out['BinNum'] = out['BinNum'].astype(int)

    return out, "OK"


# ----------------------------
# Move generation
# ----------------------------

def build_moves(df: pd.DataFrame, threshold: int):
    moves = []
    for material, group in df.groupby('Material'):
        if len(group) < 2:
            continue

        sources = group[(group['BinNum'] >= threshold) & (group['Qty'] > 0)].sort_values('BinNum', ascending=False)
        targets = group[(group['BinNum'] < threshold) & (group['Qty'] < group['Capacity'])].sort_values('BinNum', ascending=True)
        if sources.empty or targets.empty:
            continue

        tgt_qty = targets['Qty'].to_dict()

        for _, src in sources.iterrows():
            remaining = float(src['Qty'])
            if remaining <= 0:
                continue
            for t_idx in targets.index:
                tgt = targets.loc[t_idx]
                cap = float(tgt['Capacity'])
                curr = float(tgt_qty[t_idx])
                space = cap - curr
                if space <= 0:
                    continue
                # keep direction consistent: only move to lower bin numbers
                if int(tgt['BinNum']) >= int(src['BinNum']):
                    continue
                qty = min(space, remaining)
                if qty <= 0:
                    continue
                moves.append({
                    'Material': material,
                    'From': src['Bin'],
                    'To': tgt['Bin'],
                    'Qty': qty,
                    'Description': src.get('Description', '')
                })
                remaining -= qty
                tgt_qty[t_idx] = curr + qty
                if remaining <= 0:
                    break
    return moves


# ----------------------------
# GUI
# ----------------------------

class ConsolidatorApp:
    def __init__(self, root: tk.Tk) -> None:
        self.root = root
        self.root.title("Consolidator – Line Clearance")
        self.root.geometry("1000x700")

        self.file_path = tk.StringVar()
        self.threshold = tk.IntVar(value=40)
        self.status = tk.StringVar(value="Select a file to begin.")

        self.text_display = None
        self._setup_ui()

    def _setup_ui(self):
        main = ttk.Frame(self.root, padding="10")
        main.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)

        file_frame = ttk.LabelFrame(main, text="Snapshot File (XML / XLSX / HTML)", padding="10")
        file_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=6)

        ttk.Entry(file_frame, textvariable=self.file_path, width=85).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)
        ttk.Button(file_frame, text="Browse", command=self.browse_file).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)

        settings = ttk.Frame(main, padding="6")
        settings.pack(fill=tk.X)

        ttk.Label(settings, text="Empty bins with Bin# >= threshold (sources only):").pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)
        ttk.Spinbox(settings, from_=1, to=9999, increment=1, textvariable=self.threshold, width=7).pack(side=tk.LEFT)

        ttk.Button(settings, text="Generate Consolidation Plan", command=self.process_file).pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=5)
        ttk.Button(settings, text="Save Results", command=self.save_results).pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=5)

        ttk.Label(main, textvariable=self.status).pack(fill=tk.X, pady=(0, 6))

        box = ttk.LabelFrame(main, text="Moves", padding="10")
        box.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True, pady=6)

        self.text_display = tk.Text(box, wrap=tk.NONE, font=("Consolas", 10))
        vs = ttk.Scrollbar(box, orient=tk.VERTICAL, command=self.text_display.yview)
        hs = ttk.Scrollbar(box, orient=tk.HORIZONTAL, command=self.text_display.xview)
        self.text_display.configure(yscrollcommand=vs.set, xscrollcommand=hs.set)

        self.text_display.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)
        vs.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, fill=tk.Y)
        hs.pack(side=tk.BOTTOM, fill=tk.X)

    def browse_file(self):
        fn = filedialog.askopenfilename(
            filetypes=[
                ("Supported files", "*.xml *.xlsx *.xls *.htm *.html"),
                ("XML files", "*.xml"),
                ("Excel files", "*.xlsx *.xls"),
                ("HTML files", "*.htm *.html"),
                ("All files", "*.*"),
            ]
        )
        if fn:
            self.file_path.set(fn)

    def _load_snapshot(self, path: str):
        ext = path.lower().split('.')[-1] if '.' in path else ''
        try:
            if ext in ('xlsx', 'xls'):
                df = pd.read_excel(path)
                return df, "XLSX"
            if ext in ('htm', 'html'):
                df = parse_sap_html(path)
                return df, "HTML"
            if ext == 'xml':
                df = parse_xml_auto(path)
                # try to label
                head = open(path, 'rb').read(2048).decode('utf-8', errors='replace').lower()
                if '<inventoryexport' in head or '<record' in head:
                    kind = "XML (records)"
                elif 'spreadsheet' in head or '<workbook' in head:
                    kind = "XML (SpreadsheetML)"
                else:
                    kind = "XML"
                return df, kind
            raise ValueError("Unsupported file type")
        except Exception as e:
            raise

    def process_file(self):
        path = self.file_path.get().strip()
        if not path:
            return messagebox.showerror("Error", "Select a snapshot file first.")

        try:
            raw_df, kind = self._load_snapshot(path)
        except Exception as e:
            return messagebox.showerror("Error", f"Could not read file:\n{e}")

        std_df, msg = standardize_snapshot_df(raw_df)
        if std_df.empty:
            self._print(f"Could not parse snapshot.\n\n{msg}\n\n"
                        f"Tip: If this is XML, it must be SpreadsheetML or InventoryExport/Record.\n"
                        f"If this is HTML, it must include a table with StorageBin/Material.\n")
            self.status.set(f"Loaded {kind} but parsing failed.")
            return

        threshold = int(self.threshold.get())
        moves = build_moves(std_df, threshold)

        self.status.set(f"Loaded {kind} • {len(std_df)} bin records • threshold={threshold} • moves={len(moves)}")

        if not moves:
            self._print("No consolidation moves found.\n"
                        f"Either bins >= {threshold} are already empty, or bins < {threshold} have no space.\n")
            return

        lines = []
        lines.append(f"Found {len(moves)} moves. (Bins >= {threshold} are sources only)\n")
        lines.append(f"{'MATERIAL':<12} | {'FROM':<12} -> {'TO':<12} | {'QTY':>8} | DESCRIPTION")
        lines.append("-" * 100)
        for m in moves:
            lines.append(f"{m['Material']:<12} | {m['From']:<12} -> {m['To']:<12} | {m['Qty']:>8.2f} | {m.get('Description','')}")
        self._print("\n".join(lines))

    def _print(self, text: str):
        self.text_display.delete("1.0", tk.END)
        self.text_display.insert(tk.END, text)

    def save_results(self):
        txt = self.text_display.get("1.0", tk.END).strip()
        if not txt:
            return
        f = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(defaultextension=".txt", filetypes=[("Text files", "*.txt"), ("All files", "*.*")])
        if not f:
            return
        try:
            with open(f, "w", encoding="utf-8") as out:
                out.write(txt + "\n")
            messagebox.showinfo("Saved", f"Saved to:\n{f}")
        except Exception as e:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", f"Could not save:\n{e}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = tk.Tk()
    ConsolidatorApp(root)
    root.mainloop()

improved = r'''import re
import math
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox, ttk
from html.parser import HTMLParser
import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET

import pandas as pd


# ============================================================
# Core helpers
# ============================================================

def canon(s: str) -> str:
    """Lowercase + remove non-alnum for robust matching."""
    return re.sub(r'[^a-z0-9]+', '', (s or '').strip().lower())


def normalize_bin(bin_name: str):
    """
    Extract row letters + bin number dynamically (supports any row letters):
      '2A33' -> row='A',  num=33,  norm='A33'
      'AA07' -> row='AA', num=7,   norm='AA07'
      'R1'   -> row='R',  num=1,   norm='R01'
    """
    s = str(bin_name).strip()
    m = re.match(r'^(\d+)?([A-Za-z]+)(\d+)$', s)
    if not m:
        return None, None, s
    row_id = m.group(2).upper()
    num = int(m.group(3))
    return row_id, num, f"{row_id}{num:02d}"


def to_num(x, default=0.0) -> float:
    try:
        if x is None:
            return default
        if isinstance(x, float) and (math.isnan(x) or math.isinf(x)):
            return default
        s = str(x).strip()
        if s == '':
            return default
        return float(s.replace(',', ''))
    except Exception:
        return default


# ============================================================
# HTML (SAP "Report output") parser – no external deps
# ============================================================

class _SAPHTMLTableParser(HTMLParser):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.in_table = False
        self.in_tr = False
        self.in_td = False
        self.tables = []
        self._rows = []
        self._row = []
        self._cell = []

    def handle_starttag(self, tag, attrs):
        tag = tag.lower()
        if tag == 'table':
            self.in_table = True
            self._rows = []
        elif self.in_table and tag == 'tr':
            self.in_tr = True
            self._row = []
        elif self.in_table and self.in_tr and tag in ('td', 'th'):
            self.in_td = True
            self._cell = []

    def handle_endtag(self, tag):
        tag = tag.lower()
        if tag == 'table' and self.in_table:
            self.in_table = False
            if self._rows:
                self.tables.append(self._rows)
            self._rows = []
        elif tag == 'tr' and self.in_tr:
            self.in_tr = False
            if self._row:
                self._rows.append(self._row)
            self._row = []
        elif tag in ('td', 'th') and self.in_td:
            self.in_td = False
            cell_text = ''.join(self._cell).replace('\xa0', ' ')
            cell_text = re.sub(r'\s+', ' ', cell_text).strip()
            self._row.append(cell_text)
            self._cell = []

    def handle_data(self, data):
        if self.in_table and self.in_tr and self.in_td and data:
            self._cell.append(data)


def parse_sap_html(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8', errors='replace') as f:
        html = f.read()
    p = _SAPHTMLTableParser()
    p.feed(html)
    if not p.tables:
        return pd.DataFrame()

    # pick the best-looking table (prefer one with StorageBin in the header)
    best = p.tables[0]
    for t in p.tables:
        joined = ' '.join(' '.join(r) for r in t[:2]).lower()
        if 'storagebin' in joined or 'storage bin' in joined:
            best = t
            break

    if len(best) < 2:
        return pd.DataFrame()

    headers = best[0]
    data_rows = best[1:]

    fixed = []
    for r in data_rows:
        if len(r) < len(headers):
            r = r + [''] * (len(headers) - len(r))
        fixed.append(r[:len(headers)])

    return pd.DataFrame(fixed, columns=headers)


# ============================================================
# XML parsers (supports 3 formats)
#   1) Custom Record XML: <InventoryExport><Record>...</Record></InventoryExport>
#   2) SpreadsheetML "piped": rows are pipe-delimited strings inside ss:Data
#   3) SpreadsheetML "grid": Worksheet/Table/Row/Cell/Data
# ============================================================

def parse_inventoryexport_xml(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    tree = ET.parse(path)
    root = tree.getroot()
    recs = root.findall('.//Record')
    if not recs:
        return pd.DataFrame()

    rows = []
    for rec in recs:
        d = {canon(child.tag): (child.text or '').strip() for child in rec}
        rows.append(d)
    return pd.DataFrame(rows)


def parse_spreadsheetml_piped_xml(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    tree = ET.parse(path)
    root = tree.getroot()
    ns = {'ss': 'urn:schemas-microsoft-com:office:spreadsheet'}

    lines = []
    for data_node in root.findall('.//ss:Data', ns):
        t = data_node.text or ''
        if '|' not in t:
            continue
        for line in t.splitlines():
            line = line.strip()
            if line.startswith('|'):
                lines.append(line)

    if not lines:
        return pd.DataFrame()

    def split_line(l: str):
        parts = [p.strip() for p in l.split('|')]
        if parts and parts[0] == '':
            parts = parts[1:]
        if parts and parts[-1] == '':
            parts = parts[:-1]
        return parts

    header_line = None
    for l in lines[:50]:
        if 'storagebin' in l.lower():
            header_line = l
            break
    if header_line is None:
        header_line = lines[0]

    header = split_line(header_line)
    data_lines = [l for l in lines if l != header_line and '---' not in l]

    fixed = []
    for l in data_lines:
        parts = split_line(l)
        if len(parts) < len(header):
            parts = parts + [''] * (len(header) - len(parts))
        fixed.append(parts[:len(header)])

    return pd.DataFrame(fixed, columns=header)


def parse_spreadsheetml_grid_xml(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    tree = ET.parse(path)
    root = tree.getroot()
    ns = {'ss': 'urn:schemas-microsoft-com:office:spreadsheet'}

    ws = root.find('.//ss:Worksheet', ns)
    if ws is None:
        return pd.DataFrame()

    table = ws.find('.//ss:Table', ns)
    if table is None:
        return pd.DataFrame()

    rows = []
    for row in table.findall('ss:Row', ns):
        cells = []
        col_idx = 1
        for cell in row.findall('ss:Cell', ns):
            idx_attr = cell.get('{urn:schemas-microsoft-com:office:spreadsheet}Index')
            if idx_attr:
                try:
                    col_idx = int(idx_attr)
                except Exception:
                    pass

            while len(cells) < col_idx - 1:
                cells.append('')

            data = cell.find('ss:Data', ns)
            cells.append((data.text or '').strip() if data is not None else '')
            col_idx += 1

        if any(cells):
            rows.append(cells)

    if not rows:
        return pd.DataFrame()

    max_len = max(len(r) for r in rows)
    header = (rows[0] + [''] * (max_len - len(rows[0])))[:max_len]
    data_rows = []
    for r in rows[1:]:
        data_rows.append((r + [''] * (max_len - len(r)))[:max_len])

    return pd.DataFrame(data_rows, columns=header)


def parse_xml_auto(path: str):
    # peek head for fast detection
    with open(path, 'rb') as f:
        head = f.read(4096).decode('utf-8', errors='replace').lower()

    # Custom Record XML
    if '<record' in head:
        df = parse_inventoryexport_xml(path)
        if not df.empty:
            return df, "XML (records)"

    # SpreadsheetML
    if 'urn:schemas-microsoft-com:office:spreadsheet' in head or '<workbook' in head:
        df = parse_spreadsheetml_piped_xml(path)
        if not df.empty:
            return df, "XML (SpreadsheetML piped)"
        df = parse_spreadsheetml_grid_xml(path)
        if not df.empty:
            return df, "XML (SpreadsheetML grid)"

    # Fallback try record XML anyway
    df = parse_inventoryexport_xml(path)
    if not df.empty:
        return df, "XML (records)"
    return pd.DataFrame(), "XML (unknown)"


# ============================================================
# Standardize columns (works across XLSX / HTML / XML variants)
# ============================================================

def pick_bin_col(cols):
    for c in cols:
        cc = canon(str(c))
        if 'storagebin' in cc or (cc.endswith('bin') and 'storage' in cc) or cc == 'bin':
            return c
    return None


def pick_material_col(cols):
    for c in cols:
        cc = canon(str(c))
        if ('material' in cc or cc == 'materia' or cc == 'product') and ('description' not in cc):
            return c
    return None


def pick_desc_col(cols):
    for c in cols:
        cc = canon(str(c))
        if 'materialdescription' in cc or cc == 'description' or ('desc' in cc and 'material' in cc):
            return c
    return None


def pick_stock_col(cols):
    # Prefer Total Stock
    for c in cols:
        if 'totalstock' in canon(str(c)):
            return c
    # Fallback: Available stock / Qty / Quantity / Stock
    for c in cols:
        cc = canon(str(c))
        if 'availablestock' in cc or 'availstock' in cc or cc in ('qty', 'quantity', 'stock'):
            return c
    return None


def pick_capacity_col(cols):
    for c in cols:
        cc = canon(str(c))
        if 'totalcapacity' in cc:
            return c
    for c in cols:
        cc = canon(str(c))
        if 'capacity' in cc and 'remaining' not in cc:
            return c
    return None


def pick_remaining_col(cols):
    for c in cols:
        cc = canon(str(c))
        if 'remainingcapacity' in cc or ('remain' in cc and 'cap' in cc):
            return c
    return None


def standardize_snapshot_df(df: pd.DataFrame):
    if df is None or df.empty:
        return pd.DataFrame(), "No rows found"

    cols = list(df.columns)

    col_bin = pick_bin_col(cols)
    col_mat = pick_material_col(cols)
    col_desc = pick_desc_col(cols)
    col_stock = pick_stock_col(cols)
    col_cap = pick_capacity_col(cols)
    col_rem = pick_remaining_col(cols)

    if col_bin is None or col_mat is None or col_stock is None:
        return pd.DataFrame(), f"Missing required columns. Columns found: {cols}"

    out = pd.DataFrame()
    out['BinRaw'] = df[col_bin].astype(str).str.strip()
    out['Material'] = df[col_mat].astype(str).str.strip()
    out['Description'] = df[col_desc].astype(str).str.strip() if col_desc is not None else ''
    out['Qty'] = df[col_stock].apply(to_num)
    out['Capacity'] = df[col_cap].apply(to_num) if col_cap is not None else 0.0

    remaining = df[col_rem].apply(to_num) if col_rem is not None else None
    if (out['Capacity'] == 0).all() and remaining is not None and remaining.notna().any():
        out['Capacity'] = out['Qty'] + remaining

    # If still unknown capacity, treat as full (capacity=qty) so we don't route into it.
    out['Capacity'] = out.apply(lambda r: r['Capacity'] if r['Capacity'] > 0 else r['Qty'], axis=1)

    # Drop junk materials
    out = out[out['Material'].astype(str).str.strip().ne('')].copy()
    out = out[~out['Material'].str.contains('empty', case=False, na=False)].copy()

    # Normalize bins
    norm = out['BinRaw'].apply(normalize_bin)
    out['Row'] = norm.apply(lambda x: x[0])
    out['BinNum'] = norm.apply(lambda x: x[1])
    out['Bin'] = norm.apply(lambda x: x[2])
    out = out[out['BinNum'].notna()].copy()
    out['BinNum'] = out['BinNum'].astype(int)

    return out, "OK"


# ============================================================
# Move generation
# ============================================================

def build_moves(df: pd.DataFrame, threshold: int):
    moves = []
    for material, group in df.groupby('Material'):
        if len(group) < 2:
            continue

        # sources = near-line bins we want empty
        sources = group[(group['BinNum'] >= threshold) & (group['Qty'] > 0)].sort_values('BinNum', ascending=False)

        # targets = farther bins we can fill
        targets = group[(group['BinNum'] < threshold) & (group['Qty'] < group['Capacity'])].sort_values('BinNum', ascending=True)

        if sources.empty or targets.empty:
            continue

        tgt_qty = targets['Qty'].to_dict()

        for _, src in sources.iterrows():
            remaining = float(src['Qty'])
            if remaining <= 0:
                continue

            for t_idx in targets.index:
                tgt = targets.loc[t_idx]
                cap = float(tgt['Capacity'])
                curr = float(tgt_qty[t_idx])
                space = cap - curr
                if space <= 0:
                    continue

                # keep direction consistent: only move into lower bin numbers
                if int(tgt['BinNum']) >= int(src['BinNum']):
                    continue

                qty = min(space, remaining)
                if qty <= 0:
                    continue

                moves.append({
                    'Material': material,
                    'From': src['Bin'],
                    'To': tgt['Bin'],
                    'Qty': qty,
                    'Description': src.get('Description', '')
                })

                remaining -= qty
                tgt_qty[t_idx] = curr + qty

                if remaining <= 0:
                    break

    return moves


# ============================================================
# GUI
# ============================================================

class ConsolidatorApp:
    def __init__(self, root: tk.Tk) -> None:
        self.root = root
        self.root.title("Consolidator – Line Clearance")
        self.root.geometry("1000x700")

        self.file_path = tk.StringVar()
        self.threshold = tk.IntVar(value=40)
        self.status = tk.StringVar(value="Select a snapshot file to begin.")

        self.text_display = None
        self._setup_ui()

    def _setup_ui(self):
        main = ttk.Frame(self.root, padding="10")
        main.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)

        file_frame = ttk.LabelFrame(main, text="Snapshot File (XLSX / XML / HTML)", padding="10")
        file_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=6)

        ttk.Entry(file_frame, textvariable=self.file_path, width=85).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)
        ttk.Button(file_frame, text="Browse", command=self.browse_file).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)

        settings = ttk.Frame(main, padding="6")
        settings.pack(fill=tk.X)

        ttk.Label(settings, text="Empty bins with Bin# >= threshold (sources only):").pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)
        ttk.Spinbox(settings, from_=1, to=9999, increment=1, textvariable=self.threshold, width=7).pack(side=tk.LEFT)

        ttk.Button(settings, text="Generate Consolidation Plan", command=self.process_file).pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=5)
        ttk.Button(settings, text="Save Results", command=self.save_results).pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=5)

        ttk.Label(main, textvariable=self.status).pack(fill=tk.X, pady=(0, 6))

        box = ttk.LabelFrame(main, text="Moves", padding="10")
        box.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True, pady=6)

        self.text_display = tk.Text(box, wrap=tk.NONE, font=("Consolas", 10))
        vs = ttk.Scrollbar(box, orient=tk.VERTICAL, command=self.text_display.yview)
        hs = ttk.Scrollbar(box, orient=tk.HORIZONTAL, command=self.text_display.xview)
        self.text_display.configure(yscrollcommand=vs.set, xscrollcommand=hs.set)

        self.text_display.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)
        vs.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, fill=tk.Y)
        hs.pack(side=tk.BOTTOM, fill=tk.X)

    def browse_file(self):
        fn = filedialog.askopenfilename(
            filetypes=[
                ("Supported files", "*.xlsx *.xls *.xml *.htm *.html"),
                ("Excel files", "*.xlsx *.xls"),
                ("XML files", "*.xml"),
                ("HTML files", "*.htm *.html"),
                ("All files", "*.*"),
            ]
        )
        if fn:
            self.file_path.set(fn)

    def load_snapshot(self, path: str):
        ext = path.lower().split('.')[-1] if '.' in path else ''
        if ext in ('xlsx', 'xls'):
            return pd.read_excel(path), "XLSX"
        if ext in ('htm', 'html'):
            return parse_sap_html(path), "HTML"
        if ext == 'xml':
            return parse_xml_auto(path)
        raise ValueError("Unsupported file type")

    def process_file(self):
        path = self.file_path.get().strip()
        if not path:
            return messagebox.showerror("Error", "Select a snapshot file first.")

        try:
            raw_df, kind = self.load_snapshot(path)
        except Exception as e:
            return messagebox.showerror("Error", f"Could not read file:\n{e}")

        std_df, msg = standardize_snapshot_df(raw_df)
        if std_df.empty:
            self.status.set(f"Loaded {kind} but parsing failed.")
            self._print(
                "Could not parse snapshot.\n\n"
                f"{msg}\n\n"
                "Supported inputs:\n"
                "  • XLSX (SAP export)\n"
                "  • HTML (SAP 'Report output')\n"
                "  • XML (SpreadsheetML piped/grid OR InventoryExport/Record)\n"
            )
            return

        threshold = int(self.threshold.get())
        moves = build_moves(std_df, threshold)
        self.status.set(f"Loaded {kind} • {len(std_df)} bin rows • threshold={threshold} • moves={len(moves)}")

        if not moves:
            self._print(
                "No consolidation moves found.\n"
                f"Either bins >= {threshold} are already empty, or bins < {threshold} have no space.\n"
            )
            return

        lines = []
        lines.append(f"Found {len(moves)} moves. (Bins >= {threshold} are sources only)\n")
        lines.append(f"{'MATERIAL':<12} | {'FROM':<12} -> {'TO':<12} | {'QTY':>8} | DESCRIPTION")
        lines.append("-" * 100)
        for m in moves:
            lines.append(
                f"{m['Material']:<12} | {m['From']:<12} -> {m['To']:<12} | {m['Qty']:>8.2f} | {m.get('Description','')}"
            )
        self._print("\n".join(lines))

    def _print(self, text: str):
        self.text_display.delete("1.0", tk.END)
        self.text_display.insert(tk.END, text)

    def save_results(self):
        txt = self.text_display.get("1.0", tk.END).strip()
        if not txt:
            return
        f = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(
            defaultextension=".txt",
            filetypes=[("Text files", "*.txt"), ("All files", "*.*")]
        )
        if not f:
            return
        try:
            with open(f, "w", encoding="utf-8") as out:
                out.write(txt + "\n")
            messagebox.showinfo("Saved", f"Saved to:\n{f}")
        except Exception as e:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", f"Could not save:\n{e}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = tk.Tk()
    ConsolidatorApp(root)
    root.mainloop()
'''

from pathlib import Path

code = r'''import re
import math
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox, ttk
import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET

import pandas as pd

# =========================
# Bin parsing / normalization
# =========================

BIN_RE = re.compile(r'^(\d+)?([A-Za-z]+)(\d+)$')

def normalize_bin(bin_name: str):
    """
    Accepts common SAP bin formats:
      '2A33' -> row='A',  num=33,  norm='A33'
      'AA07' -> row='AA', num=7,   norm='AA07'
      'R1'   -> row='R',  num=1,   norm='R01'
    Returns (row_id, bin_num, normalized_bin_string).
    If it doesn't match letters+digits, returns (None, None, original).
    """
    s = str(bin_name).strip()
    m = BIN_RE.match(s)
    if not m:
        return None, None, s
    row_id = m.group(2).upper()
    num = int(m.group(3))
    return row_id, num, f"{row_id}{num:02d}"


# =========================
# Helpers
# =========================

def _to_float(x, default=0.0):
    try:
        if x is None:
            return default
        if isinstance(x, float) and (math.isnan(x) or math.isinf(x)):
            return default
        s = str(x).strip()
        if s == "":
            return default
        return float(s.replace(",", ""))
    except Exception:
        return default


def _pick_column(df: pd.DataFrame, *needles: str):
    """Fuzzy column picker by substring match (case-insensitive)."""
    cols = list(df.columns)
    for n in needles:
        n_l = n.lower()
        for c in cols:
            if n_l in str(c).strip().lower():
                return c
    return None


# =========================
# Parsers (XLSX / HTML / XML variants)
# =========================

def parse_xlsx(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    df = pd.read_excel(path)

    col_bin   = _pick_column(df, "storagebin", "storage bin", "bin")
    col_mat   = _pick_column(df, "materia", "material", "product")
    col_desc  = _pick_column(df, "material description", "description", "matl desc", "mat desc")
    col_stock = _pick_column(df, "total stock", "totalstock", "stock", "qty", "quantity", "avail.stock", "avail stock")
    col_cap   = _pick_column(df, "total capacity", "totalcap", "capacity", "cap", "max stock", "maxstock", "max")

    if col_bin is None or col_mat is None or col_stock is None:
        raise ValueError(
            "XLSX is missing required columns. Need at least: StorageBin/Bin, Material, Stock/Qty."
        )

    rows = []
    for _, r in df.iterrows():
        raw_bin = str(r[col_bin]).strip()
        material = str(r[col_mat]).strip()
        desc = str(r[col_desc]).strip() if col_desc is not None and pd.notna(r[col_desc]) else ""
        stock = _to_float(r[col_stock], 0.0)
        cap = _to_float(r[col_cap], 0.0) if col_cap is not None else 0.0

        row_id, bin_num, norm_bin = normalize_bin(raw_bin)
        if bin_num is None or material == "" or raw_bin == "nan":
            continue

        rows.append({
            "Material": material,
            "BinRaw": raw_bin,
            "Bin": norm_bin,
            "Row": row_id,
            "BinNum": int(bin_num),
            "Qty": float(stock),
            "Capacity": float(cap),
            "Description": desc,
        })

    return pd.DataFrame(rows)


def parse_html(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    # pandas uses lxml/html5lib under the hood; lxml is recommended.
    tables = pd.read_html(path)
    if not tables:
        raise ValueError("No tables found in HTML export.")
    # Choose the largest table by cell count
    df = max(tables, key=lambda t: t.shape[0] * t.shape[1])

    col_bin   = _pick_column(df, "storagebin", "storage bin", "bin")
    col_mat   = _pick_column(df, "materia", "material", "product")
    col_desc  = _pick_column(df, "material description", "description", "matl desc", "mat desc")
    col_stock = _pick_column(df, "total stock", "totalstock", "stock", "qty", "quantity", "avail.stock", "avail stock")
    col_cap   = _pick_column(df, "total capacity", "totalcap", "capacity", "cap", "max stock", "maxstock", "max")

    if col_bin is None or col_mat is None or col_stock is None:
        raise ValueError(
            "HTML table is missing required columns. Need at least: StorageBin/Bin, Material, Stock/Qty."
        )

    rows = []
    for _, r in df.iterrows():
        raw_bin = str(r[col_bin]).strip()
        material = str(r[col_mat]).strip()
        desc = str(r[col_desc]).strip() if col_desc is not None and pd.notna(r[col_desc]) else ""
        stock = _to_float(r[col_stock], 0.0)
        cap = _to_float(r[col_cap], 0.0) if col_cap is not None else 0.0

        row_id, bin_num, norm_bin = normalize_bin(raw_bin)
        if bin_num is None or material == "" or raw_bin.lower() == "nan":
            continue

        rows.append({
            "Material": material,
            "BinRaw": raw_bin,
            "Bin": norm_bin,
            "Row": row_id,
            "BinNum": int(bin_num),
            "Qty": float(stock),
            "Capacity": float(cap),
            "Description": desc,
        })

    return pd.DataFrame(rows)


def parse_inventoryexport_xml(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    """
    Parses XML shaped like:
      <InventoryExport>
         <Record> <StorageBin>..</StorageBin> <Material>..</Material> ... </Record>
      </InventoryExport>
    Field names vary; we try a few.
    """
    tree = ET.parse(path)
    root = tree.getroot()

    # Identify record elements (case-insensitive)
    recs = []
    for el in root.iter():
        if el.tag.lower().endswith("record"):
            recs.append(el)

    if not recs:
        raise ValueError("InventoryExport-style XML found no <Record> elements.")

    def get_text(rec, *names):
        for n in names:
            # try direct child
            child = rec.find(n)
            if child is not None and child.text:
                return child.text
            # try case-insensitive match among children
            for c in rec:
                if c.tag.lower() == n.lower() and c.text:
                    return c.text
        return ""

    rows = []
    for rec in recs:
        raw_bin = get_text(rec, "StorageBin", "Bin", "Storage_Bin").strip()
        material = get_text(rec, "Material", "Materia", "Product").strip()
        desc = get_text(rec, "MaterialDescription", "Material Description", "Description").strip()
        stock = _to_float(get_text(rec, "TotalStock", "Total Stock", "Stock", "Qty", "Quantity", "AvailStock", "Avail.stock"), 0.0)
        cap = _to_float(get_text(rec, "TotalCapacity", "Total capacity", "Capacity", "Cap", "MaxStock", "Max Stock"), 0.0)

        row_id, bin_num, norm_bin = normalize_bin(raw_bin)
        if bin_num is None or material == "":
            continue

        rows.append({
            "Material": material,
            "BinRaw": raw_bin,
            "Bin": norm_bin,
            "Row": row_id,
            "BinNum": int(bin_num),
            "Qty": float(stock),
            "Capacity": float(cap),
            "Description": desc,
        })

    return pd.DataFrame(rows)


def parse_spreadsheetml_piped_xml(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    """
    Parses SpreadsheetML where each row is a single ss:Data cell containing
    a pipe-delimited line starting with '|'.
    This matches the older SAP export / "piped" conversion.
    """
    tree = ET.parse(path)
    root = tree.getroot()
    ns = {"ss": "urn:schemas-microsoft-com:office:spreadsheet"}

    header_map = None
    rows = []

    def build_header_map(parts):
        idx = {p.strip().lower(): i for i, p in enumerate(parts) if p and p.strip()}
        def pick(*names):
            for n in names:
                i = idx.get(n.lower())
                if i is not None:
                    return i
            return None
        return {
            "bin":  pick("storagebin", "storage bin", "bin"),
            "mat":  pick("materia", "material", "product"),
            "desc": pick("material description", "description", "matl desc", "mat desc"),
            "stock":pick("total stock", "totalstock", "stock", "qty", "quantity", "avail.stock", "avail stock"),
            "cap":  pick("total capacity", "totalcap", "capacity", "cap", "max stock", "maxstock", "max"),
        }

    for data_node in root.findall(".//ss:Data", ns):
        text = data_node.text or ""
        for line in text.split("\n"):
            if not line.startswith("|"):
                continue
            if "---" in line:
                continue
            parts = [p.strip() for p in line.split("|")]

            # detect header
            lower_line = line.lower()
            if "storagebin" in lower_line and ("total stock" in lower_line or "stock" in lower_line or "qty" in lower_line):
                header_map = build_header_map(parts)
                continue

            if header_map is None:
                continue

            try:
                i_bin = header_map["bin"]
                i_mat = header_map["mat"]
                i_desc = header_map["desc"]
                i_stock = header_map["stock"]
                i_cap = header_map["cap"]

                if i_bin is None or i_mat is None or i_stock is None:
                    continue

                raw_bin = parts[i_bin] if i_bin < len(parts) else ""
                material = parts[i_mat] if i_mat < len(parts) else ""
                desc = parts[i_desc] if i_desc is not None and i_desc < len(parts) else ""
                stock_s = parts[i_stock] if i_stock < len(parts) else ""
                cap_s = parts[i_cap] if i_cap is not None and i_cap < len(parts) else ""
            except Exception:
                continue

            row_id, bin_num, norm_bin = normalize_bin(raw_bin)
            if bin_num is None or material == "":
                continue

            rows.append({
                "Material": material,
                "BinRaw": raw_bin,
                "Bin": norm_bin,
                "Row": row_id,
                "BinNum": int(bin_num),
                "Qty": _to_float(stock_s, 0.0),
                "Capacity": _to_float(cap_s, 0.0),
                "Description": desc,
            })

    df = pd.DataFrame(rows)
    if df.empty:
        raise ValueError("SpreadsheetML piped XML parsed no usable rows.")
    return df


def parse_spreadsheetml_grid_xml(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    """
    Parses SpreadsheetML grid (normal Excel 2003 XML):
      <Workbook><Worksheet><Table><Row><Cell><Data>...</Data>...
    Uses the first row as header; then maps columns by fuzzy names.
    """
    tree = ET.parse(path)
    root = tree.getroot()
    ns = {"ss": "urn:schemas-microsoft-com:office:spreadsheet"}

    table = root.find(".//ss:Worksheet/ss:Table", ns)
    if table is None:
        raise ValueError("SpreadsheetML grid XML: no <Table> found.")

    grid = []
    for row in table.findall("ss:Row", ns):
        row_vals = []
        col_index = 1
        for cell in row.findall("ss:Cell", ns):
            idx_attr = cell.attrib.get(f"{{{ns['ss']}}}Index")
            if idx_attr:
                # Fill blanks until this column
                target = int(idx_attr)
                while col_index < target:
                    row_vals.append("")
                    col_index += 1
            data = cell.find("ss:Data", ns)
            row_vals.append(data.text if data is not None and data.text is not None else "")
            col_index += 1
        grid.append(row_vals)

    if not grid or len(grid) < 2:
        raise ValueError("SpreadsheetML grid XML: not enough rows.")

    # Normalize row widths
    max_w = max(len(r) for r in grid)
    grid = [r + [""] * (max_w - len(r)) for r in grid]

    header = [str(x).strip() for x in grid[0]]
    df = pd.DataFrame(grid[1:], columns=header)

    col_bin   = _pick_column(df, "storagebin", "storage bin", "bin")
    col_mat   = _pick_column(df, "materia", "material", "product")
    col_desc  = _pick_column(df, "material description", "description", "matl desc", "mat desc")
    col_stock = _pick_column(df, "total stock", "totalstock", "stock", "qty", "quantity", "avail.stock", "avail stock")
    col_cap   = _pick_column(df, "total capacity", "totalcap", "capacity", "cap", "max stock", "maxstock", "max")

    if col_bin is None or col_mat is None or col_stock is None:
        raise ValueError("SpreadsheetML grid XML: missing required columns in header.")

    rows = []
    for _, r in df.iterrows():
        raw_bin = str(r[col_bin]).strip()
        material = str(r[col_mat]).strip()
        desc = str(r[col_desc]).strip() if col_desc is not None and pd.notna(r[col_desc]) else ""
        stock = _to_float(r[col_stock], 0.0)
        cap = _to_float(r[col_cap], 0.0) if col_cap is not None else 0.0

        row_id, bin_num, norm_bin = normalize_bin(raw_bin)
        if bin_num is None or material == "":
            continue

        rows.append({
            "Material": material,
            "BinRaw": raw_bin,
            "Bin": norm_bin,
            "Row": row_id,
            "BinNum": int(bin_num),
            "Qty": float(stock),
            "Capacity": float(cap),
            "Description": desc,
        })

    out = pd.DataFrame(rows)
    if out.empty:
        raise ValueError("SpreadsheetML grid XML parsed no usable rows.")
    return out


def parse_xml_auto(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    """
    Auto-detect:
      - InventoryExport/Record style
      - SpreadsheetML piped style (|...| lines)
      - SpreadsheetML grid style
    """
    # Quick peek at root tag without full parsing heuristics
    tree = ET.parse(path)
    root = tree.getroot()
    tag_l = root.tag.lower()

    # InventoryExport style
    if "inventoryexport" in tag_l:
        return parse_inventoryexport_xml(path)

    # SpreadsheetML
    if tag_l.endswith("workbook") or "schemas-microsoft-com:office:spreadsheet" in tag_l:
        # try piped first (it contains ss:Data with lines that start with '|')
        try:
            return parse_spreadsheetml_piped_xml(path)
        except Exception:
            return parse_spreadsheetml_grid_xml(path)

    # Fallback: try InventoryExport (many custom exports)
    try:
        return parse_inventoryexport_xml(path)
    except Exception as e:
        raise ValueError(f"Unknown XML format: {e}")


def parse_any(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    p = path.lower()
    if p.endswith(".xlsx") or p.endswith(".xls"):
        return parse_xlsx(path)
    if p.endswith(".htm") or p.endswith(".html"):
        return parse_html(path)
    if p.endswith(".xml"):
        return parse_xml_auto(path)
    raise ValueError("Unsupported file type. Supported: .xlsx/.xls, .htm/.html, .xml")


# =========================
# Consolidation algorithm
# =========================

def build_moves(df: pd.DataFrame, threshold: int):
    """
    Cross-row consolidation by Material:
      - SOURCES: BinNum >= threshold and Qty > 0  (empty near-line bins)
      - TARGETS: BinNum < threshold and Qty < Capacity (fill farther bins)
    Moves are directed from higher bin numbers to lower bin numbers.
    """
    moves = []

    # Ensure numeric
    df = df.copy()
    df["BinNum"] = pd.to_numeric(df["BinNum"], errors="coerce")
    df["Qty"] = pd.to_numeric(df["Qty"], errors="coerce").fillna(0.0)
    df["Capacity"] = pd.to_numeric(df["Capacity"], errors="coerce").fillna(0.0)

    for material, group in df.groupby("Material"):
        if len(group) < 2:
            continue

        sources = group[(group["BinNum"] >= threshold) & (group["Qty"] > 0)].sort_values("BinNum", ascending=False)
        targets = group[(group["BinNum"] < threshold) & (group["Qty"] < group["Capacity"])].sort_values("BinNum", ascending=True)

        if sources.empty or targets.empty:
            continue

        tgt_qty = targets["Qty"].to_dict()

        for _, src in sources.iterrows():
            remaining = float(src["Qty"])
            if remaining <= 0:
                continue

            for t_idx in targets.index:
                tgt = targets.loc[t_idx]
                # keep direction consistent (never move to same/higher bin number)
                if int(tgt["BinNum"]) >= int(src["BinNum"]):
                    continue

                cap = float(tgt["Capacity"])
                curr = float(tgt_qty[t_idx])
                space = cap - curr
                if space <= 0:
                    continue

                qty = min(space, remaining)
                if qty <= 0:
                    continue

                moves.append({
                    "Material": material,
                    "Description": str(src.get("Description", "")),
                    "FromBin": str(src["Bin"]),
                    "ToBin": str(tgt["Bin"]),
                    "Quantity": float(qty),
                })

                remaining -= qty
                tgt_qty[t_idx] = curr + qty
                if remaining <= 0:
                    break

    return moves


# =========================
# GUI
# =========================

class ConsolidatorApp:
    def __init__(self, root: tk.Tk):
        self.root = root
        self.root.title("Consolidator – Multi-Format Line Clearance")
        self.root.geometry("1000x700")

        self.file_path = tk.StringVar()
        self.threshold = tk.IntVar(value=40)

        self.text_display = None

        self._setup_ui()

    def _setup_ui(self):
        main = ttk.Frame(self.root, padding="10")
        main.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)

        file_frame = ttk.LabelFrame(main, text="Input Export (XLSX / HTML / XML)", padding="10")
        file_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=6)

        ttk.Entry(file_frame, textvariable=self.file_path, width=85).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)
        ttk.Button(file_frame, text="Browse", command=self.browse_file).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)

        settings = ttk.Frame(main, padding="6")
        settings.pack(fill=tk.X)

        ttk.Label(settings, text="Bins >= threshold are emptied (sources only):").pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)
        ttk.Spinbox(settings, from_=1, to=999, increment=1, textvariable=self.threshold, width=6).pack(side=tk.LEFT)

        ttk.Button(settings, text="Generate Report", command=self.process_file).pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=5)
        ttk.Button(settings, text="Save Report", command=self.save_results).pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=5)

        box = ttk.LabelFrame(main, text="Consolidation Moves", padding="10")
        box.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True, pady=6)

        self.text_display = tk.Text(box, wrap=tk.NONE, font=("Consolas", 10))
        vs = ttk.Scrollbar(box, orient=tk.VERTICAL, command=self.text_display.yview)
        hs = ttk.Scrollbar(box, orient=tk.HORIZONTAL, command=self.text_display.xview)
        self.text_display.configure(yscrollcommand=vs.set, xscrollcommand=hs.set)

        self.text_display.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)
        vs.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, fill=tk.Y)
        hs.pack(side=tk.BOTTOM, fill=tk.X)

        hint = ttk.Label(main, text="Tip: If your work laptop blocks EXEs from USB, copy Consolidator.exe to C:\\temp first.")
        hint.pack(anchor="w", pady=(4,0))

    def browse_file(self):
        fn = filedialog.askopenfilename(
            filetypes=[
                ("Supported", "*.xlsx *.xls *.xml *.htm *.html"),
                ("Excel", "*.xlsx *.xls"),
                ("XML", "*.xml"),
                ("HTML", "*.htm *.html"),
                ("All files", "*.*"),
            ]
        )
        if fn:
            self.file_path.set(fn)

    def process_file(self):
        path = self.file_path.get().strip()
        if not path:
            return messagebox.showerror("Error", "Select an export file first.")

        try:
            df = parse_any(path)

            if df.empty:
                self._print("Parsed 0 usable rows. This export may not contain bin/material/stock fields in a recognizable way.")
                return

            threshold = int(self.threshold.get())
            moves = build_moves(df, threshold)

            if not moves:
                self._print(f"No moves found.\n"
                            f"Either bins >= {threshold} are already empty, or there is no space in bins < {threshold}.")
                return

            lines = []
            lines.append(f"INPUT: {path}")
            lines.append(f"THRESHOLD: {threshold} (bins >= threshold are emptied; bins < threshold are targets)")
            lines.append(f"MOVES: {len(moves)}\n")

            lines.append(f"{'MATERIAL':<14} | {'FROM':<12} -> {'TO':<12} | {'QTY':>10} | DESCRIPTION")
            lines.append("-" * 110)

            for m in moves:
                lines.append(
                    f"{m['Material']:<14} | {m['FromBin']:<12} -> {m['ToBin']:<12} | {m['Quantity']:>10.2f} | {m['Description']}"
                )

            self._print("\n".join(lines))

        except Exception as e:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", f"Failed to process file:\n{e}")

    def _print(self, text: str):
        self.text_display.delete("1.0", tk.END)
        self.text_display.insert(tk.END, text)

    def save_results(self):
        txt = self.text_display.get("1.0", tk.END).strip()
        if not txt:
            return

        out = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(
            defaultextension=".txt",
            filetypes=[("Text files", "*.txt"), ("All files", "*.*")]
        )
        if not out:
            return

        try:
            with open(out, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                f.write(txt + "\n")
            messagebox.showinfo("Saved", f"Saved:\n{out}")
        except Exception as e:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", f"Could not save:\n{e}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = tk.Tk()
    ConsolidatorApp(root)
    root.mainloop()
