from pathlib import Path
code = r'''import re
import math
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox, ttk
import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET

import pandas as pd

# =========================
# Bin parsing / normalization
# =========================

BIN_RE = re.compile(r'^(\d+)?([A-Za-z]+)(\d+)$')

def normalize_bin(bin_name: str):
    """
    Dynamic bin parser:
      '2A33' -> row='A',  num=33,  norm='A33'
      'AA07' -> row='AA', num=7,   norm='AA07'
      'R1'   -> row='R',  num=1,   norm='R01'
    Returns (row_id, bin_num, normalized_bin_string).
    If it doesn't match letters+digits, returns (None, None, original).
    """
    s = str(bin_name).strip()
    m = BIN_RE.match(s)
    if not m:
        return None, None, s
    row_id = m.group(2).upper()
    num = int(m.group(3))
    return row_id, num, f"{row_id}{num:02d}"


# =========================
# Small utilities
# =========================

class MappingError(Exception):
    def __init__(self, message, columns=None):
        super().__init__(message)
        self.columns = columns or []

def _to_float(x, default=0.0):
    try:
        if x is None:
            return default
        if isinstance(x, float) and (math.isnan(x) or math.isinf(x)):
            return default
        s = str(x).strip()
        if s == "" or s.lower() == "nan":
            return default
        return float(s.replace(",", ""))
    except Exception:
        return default

def _pick_column_by_name(df: pd.DataFrame, *needles: str):
    cols = list(df.columns)
    for n in needles:
        n_l = n.lower()
        for c in cols:
            if n_l in str(c).strip().lower():
                return c
    return None

def _score_bin_col(series: pd.Series, sample=200):
    # score by fraction matching BIN_RE
    vals = series.dropna().astype(str).head(sample)
    if len(vals) == 0:
        return 0.0
    hits = sum(1 for v in vals if BIN_RE.match(v.strip()))
    return hits / max(1, len(vals))

def _score_numeric_col(series: pd.Series, sample=200):
    vals = series.dropna().head(sample)
    if len(vals) == 0:
        return 0.0
    nums = 0
    for v in vals:
        try:
            float(str(v).replace(",", ""))
            nums += 1
        except Exception:
            pass
    return nums / max(1, len(vals))

def _best_col_by_score(df: pd.DataFrame, scorer):
    best = None
    best_score = 0.0
    for c in df.columns:
        sc = scorer(df[c])
        if sc > best_score:
            best = c
            best_score = sc
    return best, best_score

def _find_header_row_in_sheet(df: pd.DataFrame):
    """
    For messy exports: try to detect the header row by looking for 'storage'/'bin' and 'material'
    in a row. Returns the row index (0-based) or None.
    """
    keywords = ["storage", "bin", "material", "stock", "qty", "capacity"]
    max_scan = min(50, len(df))
    best_i = None
    best_score = 0
    for i in range(max_scan):
        row = df.iloc[i].astype(str).str.lower().tolist()
        score = sum(1 for k in keywords if any(k in cell for cell in row))
        if score > best_score:
            best_score = score
            best_i = i
    return best_i if best_score >= 2 else None


# =========================
# Standardizer (raw table -> required schema)
# =========================

def standardize_table(df: pd.DataFrame, interactive_mapper=None) -> pd.DataFrame:
    """
    Converts a raw table into a normalized schema:
      Material, BinRaw, Bin, Row, BinNum, Qty, Capacity, Description
    If auto-mapping fails, calls interactive_mapper(df, required_fields) to let user choose columns.
    """
    if df is None or df.empty:
        raise MappingError("Empty table.")

    # If export has junk header lines, attempt to re-header
    if any(str(c).lower().startswith("unnamed") for c in df.columns):
        hdr_i = _find_header_row_in_sheet(df)
        if hdr_i is not None:
            new_header = df.iloc[hdr_i].tolist()
            df2 = df.iloc[hdr_i+1:].copy()
            df2.columns = [str(x).strip() for x in new_header]
            df = df2.reset_index(drop=True)

    # Auto-map by names
    col_bin   = _pick_column_by_name(df, "storagebin", "storage bin", "storage_bin", "bin")
    col_mat   = _pick_column_by_name(df, "materia", "material", "product")
    col_desc  = _pick_column_by_name(df, "material description", "description", "matl desc", "mat desc")
    col_stock = _pick_column_by_name(df, "total stock", "totalstock", "available stock", "avail.stock", "avail stock", "stock", "qty", "quantity")
    col_cap   = _pick_column_by_name(df, "total capacity", "remaining capacity", "remain.capacity", "capacity", "maxstock", "max stock", "cap", "max")

    # If missing criticals, try content-based detection
    if col_bin is None:
        col_bin, s = _best_col_by_score(df, _score_bin_col)
        if s < 0.20:
            col_bin = None

    if col_stock is None:
        col_stock, s = _best_col_by_score(df, _score_numeric_col)
        if s < 0.40:
            col_stock = None

    if col_cap is None:
        # capacity is numeric too; pick a numeric column that isn't stock if possible
        cap_candidate, s = _best_col_by_score(df, _score_numeric_col)
        if cap_candidate is not None and cap_candidate != col_stock and s >= 0.40:
            col_cap = cap_candidate

    if col_mat is None:
        # If no obvious header, pick a column with lots of non-empty strings that is NOT the bin column
        candidates = [c for c in df.columns if c != col_bin]
        best = None
        best_fill = 0
        for c in candidates:
            fill = df[c].notna().mean()
            if fill > best_fill:
                best_fill = fill
                best = c
        col_mat = best if best_fill > 0.20 else None

    required_missing = []
    if col_bin is None: required_missing.append("Bin / StorageBin")
    if col_mat is None: required_missing.append("Material")
    if col_stock is None: required_missing.append("Stock / Qty")

    if required_missing:
        if interactive_mapper is None:
            raise MappingError(
                "Couldn't auto-detect required columns: " + ", ".join(required_missing),
                columns=list(df.columns)
            )
        mapping = interactive_mapper(df, ["bin", "material", "stock", "capacity", "description"])
        col_bin   = mapping.get("bin") or col_bin
        col_mat   = mapping.get("material") or col_mat
        col_stock = mapping.get("stock") or col_stock
        col_cap   = mapping.get("capacity") or col_cap
        col_desc  = mapping.get("description") or col_desc

    if col_bin is None or col_mat is None or col_stock is None:
        raise MappingError(
            "Missing required mappings after selection. Need Bin, Material, Stock.",
            columns=list(df.columns)
        )

    rows = []
    for _, r in df.iterrows():
        raw_bin = str(r.get(col_bin, "")).strip()
        material = str(r.get(col_mat, "")).strip()
        if material.lower() == "nan": material = ""
        if raw_bin.lower() == "nan": raw_bin = ""

        if not raw_bin or not material:
            continue

        desc = ""
        if col_desc is not None:
            v = r.get(col_desc, "")
            if pd.notna(v):
                desc = str(v).strip()

        qty = _to_float(r.get(col_stock, 0.0), 0.0)
        cap = _to_float(r.get(col_cap, 0.0), 0.0) if col_cap is not None else 0.0

        row_id, bin_num, norm_bin = normalize_bin(raw_bin)
        if bin_num is None:
            continue

        rows.append({
            "Material": material,
            "BinRaw": raw_bin,
            "Bin": norm_bin,
            "Row": row_id,
            "BinNum": int(bin_num),
            "Qty": float(qty),
            "Capacity": float(cap),
            "Description": desc,
        })

    out = pd.DataFrame(rows)
    if out.empty:
        raise MappingError("Parsed rows, but none contained recognizable bins (letters+digits).")
    return out


# =========================
# Parsers
# =========================

def parse_xlsx_raw(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    # Read using pandas; if it's a weird export, headers may become Unnamed.
    return pd.read_excel(path)

def parse_html_raw(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    tables = pd.read_html(path)  # needs lxml installed for reliability
    if not tables:
        raise MappingError("No tables found in HTML export.")
    # Choose best table that likely contains the required columns/bin patterns.
    best = None
    best_score = -1
    for t in tables:
        score = 0
        cols_l = [str(c).lower() for c in t.columns]
        if any("bin" in c or "storage" in c for c in cols_l): score += 2
        if any("mater" in c for c in cols_l): score += 2
        if any("stock" in c or "qty" in c for c in cols_l): score += 2
        # bin-pattern heuristic
        bc, bs = _best_col_by_score(t, _score_bin_col)
        score += 3 if bs >= 0.25 else 0
        # size bonus
        score += min(2, (t.shape[0] * t.shape[1]) / 5000)
        if score > best_score:
            best_score = score
            best = t
    if best is None:
        raise MappingError("Could not identify a usable table in the HTML export.")
    return best

def parse_inventoryexport_raw(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    tree = ET.parse(path)
    root = tree.getroot()

    # Collect Record-like elements
    recs = []
    for el in root.iter():
        if el.tag.lower().endswith("record"):
            recs.append(el)
    if not recs:
        raise MappingError("InventoryExport-style XML found no <Record> elements.")

    # Build a dataframe from all child tags found
    dicts = []
    for rec in recs:
        d = {}
        for c in rec:
            key = c.tag.strip()
            val = c.text.strip() if c.text else ""
            d[key] = val
        dicts.append(d)
    return pd.DataFrame(dicts)

def parse_spreadsheetml_piped_raw(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    tree = ET.parse(path)
    root = tree.getroot()
    ns = {"ss": "urn:schemas-microsoft-com:office:spreadsheet"}

    # Extract all pipe lines
    lines = []
    for data_node in root.findall(".//ss:Data", ns):
        text = data_node.text or ""
        for line in text.split("\n"):
            if line.startswith("|"):
                lines.append(line)

    if not lines:
        raise MappingError("No piped lines found in SpreadsheetML.")

    # Find header line (has storage/bin + material + stock)
    header_idx = None
    for i, line in enumerate(lines[:50]):
        l = line.lower()
        if ("storage" in l or "bin" in l) and ("mater" in l) and ("stock" in l or "qty" in l):
            header_idx = i
            break

    if header_idx is None:
        # Fallback: first line is header
        header_idx = 0

    header_parts = [p.strip() for p in lines[header_idx].split("|")]
    data_lines = [ln for j, ln in enumerate(lines) if j != header_idx and "---" not in ln]

    # Normalize row widths
    data_parts = [[p.strip() for p in ln.split("|")] for ln in data_lines]
    max_w = max(len(header_parts), *(len(r) for r in data_parts)) if data_parts else len(header_parts)
    header_parts += [""] * (max_w - len(header_parts))
    data_parts = [r + [""] * (max_w - len(r)) for r in data_parts]

    df = pd.DataFrame(data_parts, columns=header_parts)
    # Remove totally blank columns
    df = df.loc[:, [c for c in df.columns if str(c).strip() != ""]]
    return df

def parse_spreadsheetml_grid_raw(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    tree = ET.parse(path)
    root = tree.getroot()
    ns = {"ss": "urn:schemas-microsoft-com:office:spreadsheet"}

    table = root.find(".//ss:Worksheet/ss:Table", ns)
    if table is None:
        raise MappingError("SpreadsheetML grid XML: no <Table> found.")

    grid = []
    for row in table.findall("ss:Row", ns):
        row_vals = []
        col_index = 1
        for cell in row.findall("ss:Cell", ns):
            idx_attr = cell.attrib.get(f"{{{ns['ss']}}}Index")
            if idx_attr:
                target = int(idx_attr)
                while col_index < target:
                    row_vals.append("")
                    col_index += 1
            data = cell.find("ss:Data", ns)
            row_vals.append(data.text if data is not None and data.text is not None else "")
            col_index += 1
        grid.append(row_vals)

    if len(grid) < 2:
        raise MappingError("SpreadsheetML grid XML: not enough rows.")

    max_w = max(len(r) for r in grid)
    grid = [r + [""] * (max_w - len(r)) for r in grid]

    # Find best header row by keywords
    best_i = 0
    best_score = -1
    keywords = ["storage", "bin", "mater", "stock", "qty", "capacity"]
    scan = min(20, len(grid))
    for i in range(scan):
        row_l = [str(x).lower() for x in grid[i]]
        score = sum(1 for k in keywords if any(k in cell for cell in row_l))
        if score > best_score:
            best_score = score
            best_i = i
    header = [str(x).strip() for x in grid[best_i]]
    data = grid[best_i+1:]

    df = pd.DataFrame(data, columns=header)
    return df

def parse_xml_raw_auto(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    tree = ET.parse(path)
    root = tree.getroot()
    tag_l = root.tag.lower()

    if "inventoryexport" in tag_l:
        return parse_inventoryexport_raw(path)

    if tag_l.endswith("workbook") or "schemas-microsoft-com:office:spreadsheet" in tag_l:
        # Try piped first
        try:
            return parse_spreadsheetml_piped_raw(path)
        except Exception:
            return parse_spreadsheetml_grid_raw(path)

    # fallback: try inventoryexport-like
    return parse_inventoryexport_raw(path)

def parse_any_to_standard(path: str, interactive_mapper=None) -> pd.DataFrame:
    p = path.lower()
    if p.endswith(".xlsx") or p.endswith(".xls"):
        raw = parse_xlsx_raw(path)
        return standardize_table(raw, interactive_mapper=interactive_mapper)
    if p.endswith(".htm") or p.endswith(".html"):
        raw = parse_html_raw(path)
        return standardize_table(raw, interactive_mapper=interactive_mapper)
    if p.endswith(".xml"):
        raw = parse_xml_raw_auto(path)
        return standardize_table(raw, interactive_mapper=interactive_mapper)
    raise MappingError("Unsupported file type. Supported: .xlsx/.xls, .htm/.html, .xml")


# =========================
# Consolidation algorithm
# =========================

def build_moves(df: pd.DataFrame, threshold: int):
    """
    Cross-row consolidation by Material:
      - SOURCES: BinNum >= threshold and Qty > 0
      - TARGETS: BinNum < threshold and Qty < Capacity
    Moves are directed from higher bin numbers to lower bin numbers.
    """
    moves = []

    df = df.copy()
    df["BinNum"] = pd.to_numeric(df["BinNum"], errors="coerce")
    df["Qty"] = pd.to_numeric(df["Qty"], errors="coerce").fillna(0.0)
    df["Capacity"] = pd.to_numeric(df["Capacity"], errors="coerce").fillna(0.0)

    for material, group in df.groupby("Material"):
        if len(group) < 2:
            continue

        sources = group[(group["BinNum"] >= threshold) & (group["Qty"] > 0)].sort_values("BinNum", ascending=False)
        targets = group[(group["BinNum"] < threshold) & (group["Qty"] < group["Capacity"])].sort_values("BinNum", ascending=True)

        if sources.empty or targets.empty:
            continue

        tgt_qty = targets["Qty"].to_dict()

        for _, src in sources.iterrows():
            remaining = float(src["Qty"])
            if remaining <= 0:
                continue

            for t_idx in targets.index:
                tgt = targets.loc[t_idx]
                if int(tgt["BinNum"]) >= int(src["BinNum"]):
                    continue

                cap = float(tgt["Capacity"])
                curr = float(tgt_qty[t_idx])
                space = cap - curr
                if space <= 0:
                    continue

                qty = min(space, remaining)
                if qty <= 0:
                    continue

                moves.append({
                    "Material": material,
                    "Description": str(src.get("Description", "")),
                    "FromBin": str(src["Bin"]),
                    "ToBin": str(tgt["Bin"]),
                    "Quantity": float(qty),
                })

                remaining -= qty
                tgt_qty[t_idx] = curr + qty
                if remaining <= 0:
                    break

    return moves


# =========================
# GUI
# =========================

class ColumnMapperDialog(tk.Toplevel):
    def __init__(self, parent, columns, required_keys):
        super().__init__(parent)
        self.title("Map Columns (one-time per file)")
        self.resizable(False, False)
        self.result = {}

        info = ttk.Label(self, text="Auto-detection failed. Pick the correct columns and click OK.")
        info.grid(row=0, column=0, columnspan=2, padx=12, pady=(12, 8), sticky="w")

        self.vars = {}
        row = 1
        for key in required_keys:
            ttk.Label(self, text=f"{key.capitalize()} column:").grid(row=row, column=0, padx=12, pady=6, sticky="e")
            v = tk.StringVar(value="")
            cb = ttk.Combobox(self, textvariable=v, values=[""] + list(columns), width=45, state="readonly")
            cb.grid(row=row, column=1, padx=12, pady=6, sticky="w")
            self.vars[key] = v
            row += 1

        btns = ttk.Frame(self)
        btns.grid(row=row, column=0, columnspan=2, padx=12, pady=(10, 12), sticky="e")

        ttk.Button(btns, text="Cancel", command=self._cancel).pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=6)
        ttk.Button(btns, text="OK", command=self._ok).pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=6)

        self.grab_set()
        self.protocol("WM_DELETE_WINDOW", self._cancel)

    def _ok(self):
        self.result = {k: v.get().strip() for k, v in self.vars.items() if v.get().strip() != ""}
        self.destroy()

    def _cancel(self):
        self.result = {}
        self.destroy()


class ConsolidatorApp:
    def __init__(self, root: tk.Tk):
        self.root = root
        self.root.title("Consolidator – Multi-Format Line Clearance (Robust)")
        self.root.geometry("1050x720")

        self.file_path = tk.StringVar()
        self.threshold = tk.IntVar(value=40)
        self.status = tk.StringVar(value="Ready.")

        self.text_display = None

        self._setup_ui()

    def _setup_ui(self):
        main = ttk.Frame(self.root, padding="10")
        main.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)

        file_frame = ttk.LabelFrame(main, text="Input Export (XLSX / HTML / XML)", padding="10")
        file_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=6)

        ttk.Entry(file_frame, textvariable=self.file_path, width=92).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)
        ttk.Button(file_frame, text="Browse", command=self.browse_file).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)

        settings = ttk.Frame(main, padding="6")
        settings.pack(fill=tk.X)

        ttk.Label(settings, text="Bins >= threshold are emptied (sources only):").pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)
        ttk.Spinbox(settings, from_=1, to=999, increment=1, textvariable=self.threshold, width=6).pack(side=tk.LEFT)

        ttk.Button(settings, text="Generate Report", command=self.process_file).pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=5)
        ttk.Button(settings, text="Save Report", command=self.save_results).pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=5)

        status_frame = ttk.Frame(main, padding=(6, 0, 6, 6))
        status_frame.pack(fill=tk.X)
        ttk.Label(status_frame, textvariable=self.status).pack(side=tk.LEFT)

        box = ttk.LabelFrame(main, text="Consolidation Moves", padding="10")
        box.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True, pady=6)

        self.text_display = tk.Text(box, wrap=tk.NONE, font=("Consolas", 10))
        vs = ttk.Scrollbar(box, orient=tk.VERTICAL, command=self.text_display.yview)
        hs = ttk.Scrollbar(box, orient=tk.HORIZONTAL, command=self.text_display.xview)
        self.text_display.configure(yscrollcommand=vs.set, xscrollcommand=hs.set)

        self.text_display.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)
        vs.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, fill=tk.Y)
        hs.pack(side=tk.BOTTOM, fill=tk.X)

        hint = ttk.Label(main, text="Tip: If your work laptop blocks EXEs from USB, copy Consolidator.exe to C:\\temp first.")
        hint.pack(anchor="w", pady=(4,0))

    def browse_file(self):
        fn = filedialog.askopenfilename(
            filetypes=[
                ("Supported", "*.xlsx *.xls *.xml *.htm *.html"),
                ("Excel", "*.xlsx *.xls"),
                ("XML", "*.xml"),
                ("HTML", "*.htm *.html"),
                ("All files", "*.*"),
            ]
        )
        if fn:
            self.file_path.set(fn)
            self.status.set("Selected file: " + fn)

    def _interactive_mapper(self, df, keys):
        dlg = ColumnMapperDialog(self.root, list(df.columns), keys)
        self.root.wait_window(dlg)
        return dlg.result

    def process_file(self):
        path = self.file_path.get().strip()
        if not path:
            return messagebox.showerror("Error", "Select an export file first.")

        try:
            self.status.set("Parsing export…")
            df = parse_any_to_standard(path, interactive_mapper=self._interactive_mapper)

            self.status.set(f"Parsed {len(df)} rows. Building moves…")

            threshold = int(self.threshold.get())
            moves = build_moves(df, threshold)

            if not moves:
                self._print(f"No moves found.\n"
                            f"Either bins >= {threshold} are already empty, or there is no space in bins < {threshold}.")
                self.status.set("No moves found.")
                return

            lines = []
            lines.append(f"INPUT: {path}")
            lines.append(f"THRESHOLD: {threshold} (bins >= threshold are emptied; bins < threshold are targets)")
            lines.append(f"MOVES: {len(moves)}\n")

            lines.append(f"{'MATERIAL':<14} | {'FROM':<12} -> {'TO':<12} | {'QTY':>10} | DESCRIPTION")
            lines.append("-" * 110)

            for m in moves:
                lines.append(
                    f"{m['Material']:<14} | {m['FromBin']:<12} -> {m['ToBin']:<12} | {m['Quantity']:>10.2f} | {m['Description']}"
                )

            self._print("\n".join(lines))
            self.status.set(f"Done. {len(moves)} moves.")

        except MappingError as e:
            self.status.set("Mapping failed.")
            msg = str(e)
            if getattr(e, "columns", None):
                msg += "\n\nColumns found:\n" + ", ".join([str(c) for c in e.columns])
            messagebox.showerror("Mapping Error", msg)
        except Exception as e:
            self.status.set("Error.")
            messagebox.showerror("Error", f"Failed to process file:\n{e}")

    def _print(self, text: str):
        self.text_display.delete("1.0", tk.END)
        self.text_display.insert(tk.END, text)

    def save_results(self):
        txt = self.text_display.get("1.0", tk.END).strip()
        if not txt:
            return

        out = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(
            defaultextension=".txt",
            filetypes=[("Text files", "*.txt"), ("All files", "*.*")]
        )
        if not out:
            return

        try:
            with open(out, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                f.write(txt + "\n")
            messagebox.showinfo("Saved", f"Saved:\n{out}")
        except Exception as e:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", f"Could not save:\n{e}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = tk.Tk()
    ConsolidatorApp(root)
    root.mainloop()

from pathlib import Path
import re

# Load previous robust script as baseline if present
base_path = Path("/mnt/data/consolidator_gui_robust.py")
if base_path.exists():
    base = base_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
else:
    # fallback to the earlier updated version name if needed
    alt = Path("/mnt/data/consolidator_gui_updated.py")
    base = alt.read_text(encoding="utf-8") if alt.exists() else ""

# We'll replace with a new full script (easier & safer than regex patching a large file).
code = r'''import re
import math
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox, ttk
import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET

import pandas as pd

# =========================
# Bin parsing / normalization
# =========================

BIN_RE = re.compile(r'^(\d+)?([A-Za-z]+)(\d+)$')

def normalize_bin(bin_name: str):
    """
    Dynamic bin parser:
      '2A33' -> row='A',  num=33,  norm='A33'
      'AA07' -> row='AA', num=7,   norm='AA07'
      'R1'   -> row='R',  num=1,   norm='R01'
    Returns (row_id, bin_num, normalized_bin_string).
    If it doesn't match letters+digits, returns (None, None, original).
    """
    s = str(bin_name).strip()
    m = BIN_RE.match(s)
    if not m:
        return None, None, s
    row_id = m.group(2).upper()
    num = int(m.group(3))
    return row_id, num, f"{row_id}{num:02d}"


# =========================
# Small utilities
# =========================

class MappingError(Exception):
    def __init__(self, message, columns=None):
        super().__init__(message)
        self.columns = columns or []

def _to_float(x, default=0.0):
    try:
        if x is None:
            return default
        if isinstance(x, float) and (math.isnan(x) or math.isinf(x)):
            return default
        s = str(x).strip()
        if s == "" or s.lower() == "nan":
            return default
        return float(s.replace(",", ""))
    except Exception:
        return default

def _pick_column_by_name(df: pd.DataFrame, *needles: str):
    cols = list(df.columns)
    for n in needles:
        n_l = n.lower()
        for c in cols:
            if n_l in str(c).strip().lower():
                return c
    return None

def _score_bin_col(series: pd.Series, sample=200):
    vals = series.dropna().astype(str).head(sample)
    if len(vals) == 0:
        return 0.0
    hits = sum(1 for v in vals if BIN_RE.match(v.strip()))
    return hits / max(1, len(vals))

def _score_numeric_col(series: pd.Series, sample=200):
    vals = series.dropna().head(sample)
    if len(vals) == 0:
        return 0.0
    nums = 0
    for v in vals:
        try:
            float(str(v).replace(",", ""))
            nums += 1
        except Exception:
            pass
    return nums / max(1, len(vals))

def _best_col_by_score(df: pd.DataFrame, scorer):
    best = None
    best_score = 0.0
    for c in df.columns:
        sc = scorer(df[c])
        if sc > best_score:
            best = c
            best_score = sc
    return best, best_score

def _find_header_row_in_sheet(df: pd.DataFrame):
    """
    For messy exports: try to detect the header row by looking for 'storage'/'bin' and 'material'
    in a row. Returns the row index (0-based) or None.
    """
    keywords = ["storage", "bin", "material", "stock", "qty", "capacity"]
    max_scan = min(50, len(df))
    best_i = None
    best_score = 0
    for i in range(max_scan):
        row = df.iloc[i].astype(str).str.lower().tolist()
        score = sum(1 for k in keywords if any(k in cell for cell in row))
        if score > best_score:
            best_score = score
            best_i = i
    return best_i if best_score >= 2 else None


# =========================
# Standardizer (raw table -> required schema)
# =========================

def standardize_table(df: pd.DataFrame, interactive_mapper=None) -> pd.DataFrame:
    """
    Converts a raw table into a normalized schema:
      Material, BinRaw, Bin, Row, BinNum, Qty, Capacity, Description

    NOTE: Capacity from the export is NOT trusted; we will override it
    later using per-Row dropdown values in the GUI.
    """
    if df is None or df.empty:
        raise MappingError("Empty table.")

    # If export has junk header lines, attempt to re-header
    if any(str(c).lower().startswith("unnamed") for c in df.columns):
        hdr_i = _find_header_row_in_sheet(df)
        if hdr_i is not None:
            new_header = df.iloc[hdr_i].tolist()
            df2 = df.iloc[hdr_i+1:].copy()
            df2.columns = [str(x).strip() for x in new_header]
            df = df2.reset_index(drop=True)

    # Auto-map by names
    col_bin   = _pick_column_by_name(df, "storagebin", "storage bin", "storage_bin", "bin")
    col_mat   = _pick_column_by_name(df, "materia", "material", "product")
    col_desc  = _pick_column_by_name(df, "material description", "description", "matl desc", "mat desc")
    col_stock = _pick_column_by_name(df, "total stock", "totalstock", "available stock", "avail.stock", "avail stock", "stock", "qty", "quantity")
    col_cap   = _pick_column_by_name(df, "total capacity", "remaining capacity", "remain.capacity", "capacity", "maxstock", "max stock", "cap", "max")

    # If missing criticals, try content-based detection
    if col_bin is None:
        col_bin, s = _best_col_by_score(df, _score_bin_col)
        if s < 0.20:
            col_bin = None

    if col_stock is None:
        col_stock, s = _best_col_by_score(df, _score_numeric_col)
        if s < 0.40:
            col_stock = None

    if col_cap is None:
        cap_candidate, s = _best_col_by_score(df, _score_numeric_col)
        if cap_candidate is not None and cap_candidate != col_stock and s >= 0.40:
            col_cap = cap_candidate

    if col_mat is None:
        candidates = [c for c in df.columns if c != col_bin]
        best = None
        best_fill = 0
        for c in candidates:
            fill = df[c].notna().mean()
            if fill > best_fill:
                best_fill = fill
                best = c
        col_mat = best if best_fill > 0.20 else None

    required_missing = []
    if col_bin is None: required_missing.append("Bin / StorageBin")
    if col_mat is None: required_missing.append("Material")
    if col_stock is None: required_missing.append("Stock / Qty")

    if required_missing:
        if interactive_mapper is None:
            raise MappingError(
                "Couldn't auto-detect required columns: " + ", ".join(required_missing),
                columns=list(df.columns)
            )
        mapping = interactive_mapper(df, ["bin", "material", "stock", "capacity", "description"])
        col_bin   = mapping.get("bin") or col_bin
        col_mat   = mapping.get("material") or col_mat
        col_stock = mapping.get("stock") or col_stock
        col_cap   = mapping.get("capacity") or col_cap
        col_desc  = mapping.get("description") or col_desc

    if col_bin is None or col_mat is None or col_stock is None:
        raise MappingError(
            "Missing required mappings after selection. Need Bin, Material, Stock.",
            columns=list(df.columns)
        )

    rows = []
    for _, r in df.iterrows():
        raw_bin = str(r.get(col_bin, "")).strip()
        material = str(r.get(col_mat, "")).strip()
        if material.lower() == "nan": material = ""
        if raw_bin.lower() == "nan": raw_bin = ""

        if not raw_bin or not material:
            continue

        desc = ""
        if col_desc is not None:
            v = r.get(col_desc, "")
            if pd.notna(v):
                desc = str(v).strip()

        qty = _to_float(r.get(col_stock, 0.0), 0.0)
        cap = _to_float(r.get(col_cap, 0.0), 0.0) if col_cap is not None else 0.0  # will be overridden

        row_id, bin_num, norm_bin = normalize_bin(raw_bin)
        if bin_num is None:
            continue

        rows.append({
            "Material": material,
            "BinRaw": raw_bin,
            "Bin": norm_bin,
            "Row": row_id,
            "BinNum": int(bin_num),
            "Qty": float(qty),
            "Capacity": float(cap),
            "Description": desc,
        })

    out = pd.DataFrame(rows)
    if out.empty:
        raise MappingError("Parsed rows, but none contained recognizable bins (letters+digits).")
    return out


# =========================
# Parsers (raw -> DataFrame)
# =========================

def parse_xlsx_raw(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    return pd.read_excel(path)

def parse_html_raw(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    tables = pd.read_html(path)  # needs lxml installed for reliability
    if not tables:
        raise MappingError("No tables found in HTML export.")
    best = None
    best_score = -1
    for t in tables:
        score = 0
        cols_l = [str(c).lower() for c in t.columns]
        if any("bin" in c or "storage" in c for c in cols_l): score += 2
        if any("mater" in c for c in cols_l): score += 2
        if any("stock" in c or "qty" in c for c in cols_l): score += 2
        bc, bs = _best_col_by_score(t, _score_bin_col)
        score += 3 if bs >= 0.25 else 0
        score += min(2, (t.shape[0] * t.shape[1]) / 5000)
        if score > best_score:
            best_score = score
            best = t
    if best is None:
        raise MappingError("Could not identify a usable table in the HTML export.")
    return best

def parse_inventoryexport_raw(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    tree = ET.parse(path)
    root = tree.getroot()
    recs = []
    for el in root.iter():
        if el.tag.lower().endswith("record"):
            recs.append(el)
    if not recs:
        raise MappingError("InventoryExport-style XML found no <Record> elements.")

    dicts = []
    for rec in recs:
        d = {}
        for c in rec:
            key = c.tag.strip()
            val = c.text.strip() if c.text else ""
            d[key] = val
        dicts.append(d)
    return pd.DataFrame(dicts)

def parse_spreadsheetml_piped_raw(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    tree = ET.parse(path)
    root = tree.getroot()
    ns = {"ss": "urn:schemas-microsoft-com:office:spreadsheet"}

    lines = []
    for data_node in root.findall(".//ss:Data", ns):
        text = data_node.text or ""
        for line in text.split("\n"):
            if line.startswith("|"):
                lines.append(line)

    if not lines:
        raise MappingError("No piped lines found in SpreadsheetML.")

    header_idx = None
    for i, line in enumerate(lines[:50]):
        l = line.lower()
        if ("storage" in l or "bin" in l) and ("mater" in l) and ("stock" in l or "qty" in l):
            header_idx = i
            break
    if header_idx is None:
        header_idx = 0

    header_parts = [p.strip() for p in lines[header_idx].split("|")]
    data_lines = [ln for j, ln in enumerate(lines) if j != header_idx and "---" not in ln]

    data_parts = [[p.strip() for p in ln.split("|")] for ln in data_lines]
    max_w = max(len(header_parts), *(len(r) for r in data_parts)) if data_parts else len(header_parts)
    header_parts += [""] * (max_w - len(header_parts))
    data_parts = [r + [""] * (max_w - len(r)) for r in data_parts]

    df = pd.DataFrame(data_parts, columns=header_parts)
    df = df.loc[:, [c for c in df.columns if str(c).strip() != ""]]
    return df

def parse_spreadsheetml_grid_raw(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    tree = ET.parse(path)
    root = tree.getroot()
    ns = {"ss": "urn:schemas-microsoft-com:office:spreadsheet"}

    table = root.find(".//ss:Worksheet/ss:Table", ns)
    if table is None:
        raise MappingError("SpreadsheetML grid XML: no <Table> found.")

    grid = []
    for row in table.findall("ss:Row", ns):
        row_vals = []
        col_index = 1
        for cell in row.findall("ss:Cell", ns):
            idx_attr = cell.attrib.get(f"{{{ns['ss']}}}Index")
            if idx_attr:
                target = int(idx_attr)
                while col_index < target:
                    row_vals.append("")
                    col_index += 1
            data = cell.find("ss:Data", ns)
            row_vals.append(data.text if data is not None and data.text is not None else "")
            col_index += 1
        grid.append(row_vals)

    if len(grid) < 2:
        raise MappingError("SpreadsheetML grid XML: not enough rows.")

    max_w = max(len(r) for r in grid)
    grid = [r + [""] * (max_w - len(r)) for r in grid]

    keywords = ["storage", "bin", "mater", "stock", "qty", "capacity"]
    best_i = 0
    best_score = -1
    scan = min(20, len(grid))
    for i in range(scan):
        row_l = [str(x).lower() for x in grid[i]]
        score = sum(1 for k in keywords if any(k in cell for cell in row_l))
        if score > best_score:
            best_score = score
            best_i = i

    header = [str(x).strip() for x in grid[best_i]]
    data = grid[best_i+1:]
    return pd.DataFrame(data, columns=header)

def parse_xml_raw_auto(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    tree = ET.parse(path)
    root = tree.getroot()
    tag_l = root.tag.lower()

    if "inventoryexport" in tag_l:
        return parse_inventoryexport_raw(path)

    if tag_l.endswith("workbook") or "schemas-microsoft-com:office:spreadsheet" in tag_l:
        try:
            return parse_spreadsheetml_piped_raw(path)
        except Exception:
            return parse_spreadsheetml_grid_raw(path)

    return parse_inventoryexport_raw(path)

def parse_any_to_standard(path: str, interactive_mapper=None) -> pd.DataFrame:
    p = path.lower()
    if p.endswith(".xlsx") or p.endswith(".xls"):
        return standardize_table(parse_xlsx_raw(path), interactive_mapper=interactive_mapper)
    if p.endswith(".htm") or p.endswith(".html"):
        return standardize_table(parse_html_raw(path), interactive_mapper=interactive_mapper)
    if p.endswith(".xml"):
        return standardize_table(parse_xml_raw_auto(path), interactive_mapper=interactive_mapper)
    raise MappingError("Unsupported file type. Supported: .xlsx/.xls, .htm/.html, .xml")


# =========================
# Consolidation algorithm
# =========================

def build_moves(df: pd.DataFrame, threshold: int):
    """
    Cross-row consolidation by Material:
      - SOURCES: BinNum >= threshold and Qty > 0
      - TARGETS: BinNum < threshold and Qty < Capacity
    Moves are directed from higher bin numbers to lower bin numbers.
    """
    moves = []

    df = df.copy()
    df["BinNum"] = pd.to_numeric(df["BinNum"], errors="coerce")
    df["Qty"] = pd.to_numeric(df["Qty"], errors="coerce").fillna(0.0)
    df["Capacity"] = pd.to_numeric(df["Capacity"], errors="coerce").fillna(0.0)

    for material, group in df.groupby("Material"):
        if len(group) < 2:
            continue

        sources = group[(group["BinNum"] >= threshold) & (group["Qty"] > 0)].sort_values("BinNum", ascending=False)
        targets = group[(group["BinNum"] < threshold) & (group["Qty"] < group["Capacity"])].sort_values("BinNum", ascending=True)

        if sources.empty or targets.empty:
            continue

        tgt_qty = targets["Qty"].to_dict()

        for _, src in sources.iterrows():
            remaining = float(src["Qty"])
            if remaining <= 0:
                continue

            for t_idx in targets.index:
                tgt = targets.loc[t_idx]
                if int(tgt["BinNum"]) >= int(src["BinNum"]):
                    continue

                cap = float(tgt["Capacity"])
                curr = float(tgt_qty[t_idx])
                space = cap - curr
                if space <= 0:
                    continue

                qty = min(space, remaining)
                if qty <= 0:
                    continue

                moves.append({
                    "Material": material,
                    "Description": str(src.get("Description", "")),
                    "FromBin": str(src["Bin"]),
                    "ToBin": str(tgt["Bin"]),
                    "Quantity": float(qty),
                })

                remaining -= qty
                tgt_qty[t_idx] = curr + qty
                if remaining <= 0:
                    break

    return moves


# =========================
# GUI widgets
# =========================

class ColumnMapperDialog(tk.Toplevel):
    def __init__(self, parent, columns, required_keys):
        super().__init__(parent)
        self.title("Map Columns (one-time per file)")
        self.resizable(False, False)
        self.result = {}

        info = ttk.Label(self, text="Auto-detection failed. Pick the correct columns and click OK.")
        info.grid(row=0, column=0, columnspan=2, padx=12, pady=(12, 8), sticky="w")

        self.vars = {}
        row = 1
        for key in required_keys:
            ttk.Label(self, text=f"{key.capitalize()} column:").grid(row=row, column=0, padx=12, pady=6, sticky="e")
            v = tk.StringVar(value="")
            cb = ttk.Combobox(self, textvariable=v, values=[""] + list(columns), width=45, state="readonly")
            cb.grid(row=row, column=1, padx=12, pady=6, sticky="w")
            self.vars[key] = v
            row += 1

        btns = ttk.Frame(self)
        btns.grid(row=row, column=0, columnspan=2, padx=12, pady=(10, 12), sticky="e")

        ttk.Button(btns, text="Cancel", command=self._cancel).pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=6)
        ttk.Button(btns, text="OK", command=self._ok).pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=6)

        self.grab_set()
        self.protocol("WM_DELETE_WINDOW", self._cancel)

    def _ok(self):
        self.result = {k: v.get().strip() for k, v in self.vars.items() if v.get().strip() != ""}
        self.destroy()

    def _cancel(self):
        self.result = {}
        self.destroy()


class ScrollFrame(ttk.Frame):
    """Simple scrollable frame (vertical)."""
    def __init__(self, parent):
        super().__init__(parent)
        canvas = tk.Canvas(self, highlightthickness=0)
        vsb = ttk.Scrollbar(self, orient="vertical", command=canvas.yview)
        self.inner = ttk.Frame(canvas)

        self.inner.bind(
            "<Configure>",
            lambda e: canvas.configure(scrollregion=canvas.bbox("all"))
        )
        canvas.create_window((0, 0), window=self.inner, anchor="nw")
        canvas.configure(yscrollcommand=vsb.set)

        canvas.pack(side="left", fill="both", expand=True)
        vsb.pack(side="right", fill="y")

        # mousewheel support
        def _on_mousewheel(event):
            try:
                canvas.yview_scroll(int(-1*(event.delta/120)), "units")
            except Exception:
                pass
        canvas.bind_all("<MouseWheel>", _on_mousewheel)

# Main App
# =========================

class ConsolidatorApp:
    def __init__(self, root: tk.Tk):
        self.root = root
        self.root.title("Consolidator – Multi-Format Line Clearance (Row Capacity Override)")
        self.root.geometry("1200x760")

        self.file_path = tk.StringVar()
        self.threshold = tk.IntVar(value=40)
        self.status = tk.StringVar(value="Ready.")

        # Row capacity dropdowns (no defaults)
        self.row_capacity_vars = {}  # row_id -> StringVar
        self.current_rows_signature = None

        self.text_display = None
        self.row_cap_scroll = None

        self._setup_ui()

    def _setup_ui(self):
        main = ttk.Frame(self.root, padding="10")
        main.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)

        top = ttk.Frame(main)
        top.pack(fill=tk.X)

        file_frame = ttk.LabelFrame(top, text="Input Export (XLSX / HTML / XML)", padding="10")
        file_frame.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.X, expand=True, pady=6)

        ttk.Entry(file_frame, textvariable=self.file_path, width=90).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)
        ttk.Button(file_frame, text="Browse", command=self.browse_file).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)

        controls = ttk.LabelFrame(top, text="Controls", padding="10")
        controls.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, fill=tk.Y, padx=(10,0), pady=6)

        ttk.Label(controls, text="Threshold (bins >= are sources):").pack(anchor="w")
        ttk.Spinbox(controls, from_=1, to=999, increment=1, textvariable=self.threshold, width=8).pack(anchor="w", pady=(0,8))

        ttk.Button(controls, text="Generate Report", command=self.process_file).pack(fill=tk.X, pady=(0,6))
        ttk.Button(controls, text="Save Report", command=self.save_results).pack(fill=tk.X)

        ttk.Label(main, textvariable=self.status).pack(anchor="w", pady=(2,8))

        mid = ttk.Frame(main)
        mid.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)

        # Row capacity panel (left)
        rowcap = ttk.LabelFrame(mid, text="Row Bin Capacity Overrides (required)", padding="10")
        rowcap.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.Y, padx=(0,10))

        ttk.Label(rowcap, text="Set capacity per Row (2–45). No defaults.\nReport won't run until all rows are set.").pack(anchor="w", pady=(0,8))

        self.row_cap_scroll = ScrollFrame(rowcap)
        self.row_cap_scroll.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)

        # Results panel (right)
        box = ttk.LabelFrame(mid, text="Consolidation Moves", padding="10")
        box.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)

        self.text_display = tk.Text(box, wrap=tk.NONE, font=("Consolas", 10))
        vs = ttk.Scrollbar(box, orient=tk.VERTICAL, command=self.text_display.yview)
        hs = ttk.Scrollbar(box, orient=tk.HORIZONTAL, command=self.text_display.xview)
        self.text_display.configure(yscrollcommand=vs.set, xscrollcommand=hs.set)

        self.text_display.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)
        vs.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, fill=tk.Y)
        hs.pack(side=tk.BOTTOM, fill=tk.X)

        hint = ttk.Label(main, text="Tip: If your work laptop blocks EXEs from USB, copy Consolidator.exe to C:\\temp first.")
        hint.pack(anchor="w", pady=(6,0))

    def browse_file(self):
        fn = filedialog.askopenfilename(
            filetypes=[
                ("Supported", "*.xlsx *.xls *.xml *.htm *.html"),
                ("Excel", "*.xlsx *.xls"),
                ("XML", "*.xml"),
                ("HTML", "*.htm *.html"),
                ("All files", "*.*"),
            ]
        )
        if fn:
            self.file_path.set(fn)
            self.status.set("Selected file: " + fn)
            # clear row capacity UI; will repopulate on Generate
            self._reset_row_capacities()

    def _reset_row_capacities(self):
        self.row_capacity_vars = {}
        self.current_rows_signature = None
        # clear scrollframe widgets
        for child in self.row_cap_scroll.inner.winfo_children():
            child.destroy()

    def _interactive_mapper(self, df, keys):
        dlg = ColumnMapperDialog(self.root, list(df.columns), keys)
        self.root.wait_window(dlg)
        return dlg.result

    def _ensure_row_capacity_controls(self, rows):
        """
        Build (or update) per-row dropdowns for capacities.
        rows: list of row_ids (strings)
        """
        signature = ",".join(rows)
        if signature == self.current_rows_signature:
            return  # already built

        # reset and rebuild
        for child in self.row_cap_scroll.inner.winfo_children():
            child.destroy()

        self.row_capacity_vars = {}
        self.current_rows_signature = signature

        values = [str(i) for i in range(2, 46)]  # 2–45 inclusive

        for i, row_id in enumerate(rows):
            fr = ttk.Frame(self.row_cap_scroll.inner)
            fr.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=2)

            ttk.Label(fr, text=f"Row {row_id}:", width=10).pack(side=tk.LEFT)

            v = tk.StringVar(value="")  # no default
            cb = ttk.Combobox(fr, textvariable=v, values=values, width=8, state="readonly")
            cb.pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=6)

            self.row_capacity_vars[row_id] = v

    def _apply_row_capacities(self, df: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """
        Overrides df['Capacity'] with the per-row values.
        Enforces that all rows present in df have a capacity selected (no defaults).
        """
        rows = sorted([r for r in df["Row"].dropna().unique() if str(r).strip() != ""])
        rows = [str(r) for r in rows]
        self._ensure_row_capacity_controls(rows)

        missing = [r for r in rows if self.row_capacity_vars.get(r) is None or self.row_capacity_vars[r].get().strip() == ""]
        if missing:
            # Don't run. Force user to pick capacities first.
            messagebox.showerror(
                "Row capacities required",
                "Set capacity (2–45) for these rows first:\n" + ", ".join(missing)
            )
            raise MappingError("Row capacity not set for all rows.")

        cap_map = {r: float(self.row_capacity_vars[r].get().strip()) for r in rows}
        df = df.copy()
        df["Capacity"] = df["Row"].astype(str).map(lambda r: cap_map.get(r, 0.0))
        return df

    def process_file(self):
        path = self.file_path.get().strip()
        if not path:
            return messagebox.showerror("Error", "Select an export file first.")

        try:
            self.status.set("Parsing export…")
            df = parse_any_to_standard(path, interactive_mapper=self._interactive_mapper)

            if df.empty:
                self._print("Parsed 0 usable rows.")
                self.status.set("Parsed 0 rows.")
                return

            # Override capacity using dropdowns
            df = self._apply_row_capacities(df)

            self.status.set(f"Parsed {len(df)} rows. Building moves…")

            threshold = int(self.threshold.get())
            moves = build_moves(df, threshold)

            if not moves:
                self._print(f"No moves found.\n"
                            f"Either bins >= {threshold} are already empty, or there is no space in bins < {threshold} (using your row capacities).")
                self.status.set("No moves found.")
                return

            lines = []
            lines.append(f"INPUT: {path}")
            lines.append(f"THRESHOLD: {threshold} (bins >= threshold are emptied; bins < threshold are targets)")
            lines.append("CAPACITY OVERRIDE: per-row dropdowns (2–45)")
            lines.append(f"MOVES: {len(moves)}\n")

            lines.append(f"{'MATERIAL':<14} | {'FROM':<12} -> {'TO':<12} | {'QTY':>10} | DESCRIPTION")
            lines.append("-" * 110)

            for m in moves:
                lines.append(
                    f"{m['Material']:<14} | {m['FromBin']:<12} -> {m['ToBin']:<12} | {m['Quantity']:>10.2f} | {m['Description']}"
                )

            self._print("\n".join(lines))
            self.status.set(f"Done. {len(moves)} moves.")

        except MappingError:
            # already messaged (or deliberate stop)
            self.status.set("Needs row capacities / mapping.")
        except Exception as e:
            self.status.set("Error.")
            messagebox.showerror("Error", f"Failed to process file:\n{e}")

    def _print(self, text: str):
        self.text_display.delete("1.0", tk.END)
        self.text_display.insert(tk.END, text)

    def save_results(self):
        txt = self.text_display.get("1.0", tk.END).strip()
        if not txt:
            return

        out = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(
            defaultextension=".txt",
            filetypes=[("Text files", "*.txt"), ("All files", "*.*")]
        )
        if not out:
            return

        try:
            with open(out, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                f.write(txt + "\n")
            messagebox.showinfo("Saved", f"Saved:\n{out}")
        except Exception as e:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", f"Could not save:\n{e}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = tk.Tk()
    ConsolidatorApp(root)
    root.mainloop()

from pathlib import Path

code = r'''import re
import math
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox, ttk
import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET

import pandas as pd

# =========================
# Bin parsing / normalization
# =========================

BIN_RE = re.compile(r'^(\d+)?([A-Za-z]+)(\d+)$')

def normalize_bin(bin_name: str):
    """
    Dynamic bin parser:
      '2A33' -> row='A',  num=33,  norm='A33'
      'AA07' -> row='AA', num=7,   norm='AA07'
      'R1'   -> row='R',  num=1,   norm='R01'
    Returns (row_id, bin_num, normalized_bin_string).
    If it doesn't match letters+digits, returns (None, None, original).
    """
    s = str(bin_name).strip()
    m = BIN_RE.match(s)
    if not m:
        return None, None, s
    row_id = m.group(2).upper()
    num = int(m.group(3))
    return row_id, num, f"{row_id}{num:02d}"


# =========================
# Small utilities
# =========================

class MappingError(Exception):
    def __init__(self, message, columns=None):
        super().__init__(message)
        self.columns = columns or []

def _to_float(x, default=0.0):
    try:
        if x is None:
            return default
        if isinstance(x, float) and (math.isnan(x) or math.isinf(x)):
            return default
        s = str(x).strip()
        if s == "" or s.lower() == "nan":
            return default
        return float(s.replace(",", ""))
    except Exception:
        return default

def _pick_column_by_name(df: pd.DataFrame, *needles: str):
    cols = list(df.columns)
    for n in needles:
        n_l = n.lower()
        for c in cols:
            if n_l in str(c).strip().lower():
                return c
    return None

def _score_bin_col(series: pd.Series, sample=200):
    vals = series.dropna().astype(str).head(sample)
    if len(vals) == 0:
        return 0.0
    hits = sum(1 for v in vals if BIN_RE.match(v.strip()))
    return hits / max(1, len(vals))

def _score_numeric_col(series: pd.Series, sample=200):
    vals = series.dropna().head(sample)
    if len(vals) == 0:
        return 0.0
    nums = 0
    for v in vals:
        try:
            float(str(v).replace(",", ""))
            nums += 1
        except Exception:
            pass
    return nums / max(1, len(vals))

def _best_col_by_score(df: pd.DataFrame, scorer):
    best = None
    best_score = 0.0
    for c in df.columns:
        sc = scorer(df[c])
        if sc > best_score:
            best = c
            best_score = sc
    return best, best_score

def _find_header_row_in_sheet(df: pd.DataFrame):
    keywords = ["storage", "bin", "material", "stock", "qty", "capacity"]
    max_scan = min(50, len(df))
    best_i = None
    best_score = 0
    for i in range(max_scan):
        row = df.iloc[i].astype(str).str.lower().tolist()
        score = sum(1 for k in keywords if any(k in cell for cell in row))
        if score > best_score:
            best_score = score
            best_i = i
    return best_i if best_score >= 2 else None


# =========================
# Standardizer (raw table -> required schema)
# =========================

def standardize_table(df: pd.DataFrame, interactive_mapper=None) -> pd.DataFrame:
    """
    Converts a raw table into a normalized schema:
      Material, BinRaw, Bin, Row, BinNum, Qty, Capacity, Description

    NOTE: Capacity from the export is NOT trusted; we will override it
    later using per-Row dropdown values in the GUI.
    """
    if df is None or df.empty:
        raise MappingError("Empty table.")

    # If export has junk header lines, attempt to re-header
    if any(str(c).lower().startswith("unnamed") for c in df.columns):
        hdr_i = _find_header_row_in_sheet(df)
        if hdr_i is not None:
            new_header = df.iloc[hdr_i].tolist()
            df2 = df.iloc[hdr_i+1:].copy()
            df2.columns = [str(x).strip() for x in new_header]
            df = df2.reset_index(drop=True)

    # Auto-map by names
    col_bin   = _pick_column_by_name(df, "storagebin", "storage bin", "storage_bin", "bin")
    col_mat   = _pick_column_by_name(df, "materia", "material", "product")
    col_desc  = _pick_column_by_name(df, "material description", "description", "matl desc", "mat desc")
    col_stock = _pick_column_by_name(df, "total stock", "totalstock", "available stock", "avail.stock", "avail stock", "stock", "qty", "quantity")
    col_cap   = _pick_column_by_name(df, "total capacity", "remaining capacity", "remain.capacity", "capacity", "maxstock", "max stock", "cap", "max")

    # If missing criticals, try content-based detection
    if col_bin is None:
        col_bin, s = _best_col_by_score(df, _score_bin_col)
        if s < 0.20:
            col_bin = None

    if col_stock is None:
        col_stock, s = _best_col_by_score(df, _score_numeric_col)
        if s < 0.40:
            col_stock = None

    if col_cap is None:
        cap_candidate, s = _best_col_by_score(df, _score_numeric_col)
        if cap_candidate is not None and cap_candidate != col_stock and s >= 0.40:
            col_cap = cap_candidate

    if col_mat is None:
        candidates = [c for c in df.columns if c != col_bin]
        best = None
        best_fill = 0
        for c in candidates:
            fill = df[c].notna().mean()
            if fill > best_fill:
                best_fill = fill
                best = c
        col_mat = best if best_fill > 0.20 else None

    required_missing = []
    if col_bin is None: required_missing.append("Bin / StorageBin")
    if col_mat is None: required_missing.append("Material")
    if col_stock is None: required_missing.append("Stock / Qty")

    if required_missing:
        if interactive_mapper is None:
            raise MappingError(
                "Couldn't auto-detect required columns: " + ", ".join(required_missing),
                columns=list(df.columns)
            )
        mapping = interactive_mapper(df, ["bin", "material", "stock", "capacity", "description"])
        col_bin   = mapping.get("bin") or col_bin
        col_mat   = mapping.get("material") or col_mat
        col_stock = mapping.get("stock") or col_stock
        col_cap   = mapping.get("capacity") or col_cap
        col_desc  = mapping.get("description") or col_desc

    if col_bin is None or col_mat is None or col_stock is None:
        raise MappingError(
            "Missing required mappings after selection. Need Bin, Material, Stock.",
            columns=list(df.columns)
        )

    rows = []
    for _, r in df.iterrows():
        raw_bin = str(r.get(col_bin, "")).strip()
        material = str(r.get(col_mat, "")).strip()
        if material.lower() == "nan": material = ""
        if raw_bin.lower() == "nan": raw_bin = ""

        if not raw_bin or not material:
            continue

        desc = ""
        if col_desc is not None:
            v = r.get(col_desc, "")
            if pd.notna(v):
                desc = str(v).strip()

        qty = _to_float(r.get(col_stock, 0.0), 0.0)
        cap = _to_float(r.get(col_cap, 0.0), 0.0) if col_cap is not None else 0.0  # overridden later

        row_id, bin_num, norm_bin = normalize_bin(raw_bin)
        if bin_num is None:
            continue

        rows.append({
            "Material": material,
            "BinRaw": raw_bin,
            "Bin": norm_bin,
            "Row": row_id,
            "BinNum": int(bin_num),
            "Qty": float(qty),
            "Capacity": float(cap),
            "Description": desc,
        })

    out = pd.DataFrame(rows)
    if out.empty:
        raise MappingError("Parsed rows, but none contained recognizable bins (letters+digits).")
    return out


# =========================
# Parsers (raw -> DataFrame)
# =========================

def parse_xlsx_raw(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    return pd.read_excel(path)

def parse_html_raw(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    tables = pd.read_html(path)  # needs lxml installed for reliability
    if not tables:
        raise MappingError("No tables found in HTML export.")
    best = None
    best_score = -1
    for t in tables:
        score = 0
        cols_l = [str(c).lower() for c in t.columns]
        if any("bin" in c or "storage" in c for c in cols_l): score += 2
        if any("mater" in c for c in cols_l): score += 2
        if any("stock" in c or "qty" in c for c in cols_l): score += 2
        bc, bs = _best_col_by_score(t, _score_bin_col)
        score += 3 if bs >= 0.25 else 0
        score += min(2, (t.shape[0] * t.shape[1]) / 5000)
        if score > best_score:
            best_score = score
            best = t
    if best is None:
        raise MappingError("Could not identify a usable table in the HTML export.")
    return best

def parse_inventoryexport_raw(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    tree = ET.parse(path)
    root = tree.getroot()
    recs = []
    for el in root.iter():
        if el.tag.lower().endswith("record"):
            recs.append(el)
    if not recs:
        raise MappingError("InventoryExport-style XML found no <Record> elements.")

    dicts = []
    for rec in recs:
        d = {}
        for c in rec:
            key = c.tag.strip()
            val = c.text.strip() if c.text else ""
            d[key] = val
        dicts.append(d)
    return pd.DataFrame(dicts)

def parse_spreadsheetml_piped_raw(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    tree = ET.parse(path)
    root = tree.getroot()
    ns = {"ss": "urn:schemas-microsoft-com:office:spreadsheet"}

    lines = []
    for data_node in root.findall(".//ss:Data", ns):
        text = data_node.text or ""
        for line in text.split("\n"):
            if line.startswith("|"):
                lines.append(line)

    if not lines:
        raise MappingError("No piped lines found in SpreadsheetML.")

    header_idx = None
    for i, line in enumerate(lines[:50]):
        l = line.lower()
        if ("storage" in l or "bin" in l) and ("mater" in l) and ("stock" in l or "qty" in l):
            header_idx = i
            break
    if header_idx is None:
        header_idx = 0

    header_parts = [p.strip() for p in lines[header_idx].split("|")]
    data_lines = [ln for j, ln in enumerate(lines) if j != header_idx and "---" not in ln]

    data_parts = [[p.strip() for p in ln.split("|")] for ln in data_lines]
    max_w = max(len(header_parts), *(len(r) for r in data_parts)) if data_parts else len(header_parts)
    header_parts += [""] * (max_w - len(header_parts))
    data_parts = [r + [""] * (max_w - len(r)) for r in data_parts]

    df = pd.DataFrame(data_parts, columns=header_parts)
    df = df.loc[:, [c for c in df.columns if str(c).strip() != ""]]
    return df

def parse_spreadsheetml_grid_raw(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    tree = ET.parse(path)
    root = tree.getroot()
    ns = {"ss": "urn:schemas-microsoft-com:office:spreadsheet"}

    table = root.find(".//ss:Worksheet/ss:Table", ns)
    if table is None:
        raise MappingError("SpreadsheetML grid XML: no <Table> found.")

    grid = []
    for row in table.findall("ss:Row", ns):
        row_vals = []
        col_index = 1
        for cell in row.findall("ss:Cell", ns):
            idx_attr = cell.attrib.get(f"{{{ns['ss']}}}Index")
            if idx_attr:
                target = int(idx_attr)
                while col_index < target:
                    row_vals.append("")
                    col_index += 1
            data = cell.find("ss:Data", ns)
            row_vals.append(data.text if data is not None and data.text is not None else "")
            col_index += 1
        grid.append(row_vals)

    if len(grid) < 2:
        raise MappingError("SpreadsheetML grid XML: not enough rows.")

    max_w = max(len(r) for r in grid)
    grid = [r + [""] * (max_w - len(r)) for r in grid]

    keywords = ["storage", "bin", "mater", "stock", "qty", "capacity"]
    best_i = 0
    best_score = -1
    scan = min(20, len(grid))
    for i in range(scan):
        row_l = [str(x).lower() for x in grid[i]]
        score = sum(1 for k in keywords if any(k in cell for cell in row_l))
        if score > best_score:
            best_score = score
            best_i = i

    header = [str(x).strip() for x in grid[best_i]]
    data = grid[best_i+1:]
    return pd.DataFrame(data, columns=header)

def parse_xml_raw_auto(path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    tree = ET.parse(path)
    root = tree.getroot()
    tag_l = root.tag.lower()

    if "inventoryexport" in tag_l:
        return parse_inventoryexport_raw(path)

    if tag_l.endswith("workbook") or "schemas-microsoft-com:office:spreadsheet" in tag_l:
        try:
            return parse_spreadsheetml_piped_raw(path)
        except Exception:
            return parse_spreadsheetml_grid_raw(path)

    return parse_inventoryexport_raw(path)

def parse_any_to_standard(path: str, interactive_mapper=None) -> pd.DataFrame:
    p = path.lower()
    if p.endswith(".xlsx") or p.endswith(".xls"):
        return standardize_table(parse_xlsx_raw(path), interactive_mapper=interactive_mapper)
    if p.endswith(".htm") or p.endswith(".html"):
        return standardize_table(parse_html_raw(path), interactive_mapper=interactive_mapper)
    if p.endswith(".xml"):
        return standardize_table(parse_xml_raw_auto(path), interactive_mapper=interactive_mapper)
    raise MappingError("Unsupported file type. Supported: .xlsx/.xls, .htm/.html, .xml")


# =========================
# Consolidation algorithm
# =========================

def build_moves(df: pd.DataFrame, threshold: int):
    moves = []

    df = df.copy()
    df["BinNum"] = pd.to_numeric(df["BinNum"], errors="coerce")
    df["Qty"] = pd.to_numeric(df["Qty"], errors="coerce").fillna(0.0)
    df["Capacity"] = pd.to_numeric(df["Capacity"], errors="coerce").fillna(0.0)

    for material, group in df.groupby("Material"):
        if len(group) < 2:
            continue

        sources = group[(group["BinNum"] >= threshold) & (group["Qty"] > 0)].sort_values("BinNum", ascending=False)
        targets = group[(group["BinNum"] < threshold) & (group["Qty"] < group["Capacity"])].sort_values("BinNum", ascending=True)

        if sources.empty or targets.empty:
            continue

        tgt_qty = targets["Qty"].to_dict()

        for _, src in sources.iterrows():
            remaining = float(src["Qty"])
            if remaining <= 0:
                continue

            for t_idx in targets.index:
                tgt = targets.loc[t_idx]
                if int(tgt["BinNum"]) >= int(src["BinNum"]):
                    continue

                cap = float(tgt["Capacity"])
                curr = float(tgt_qty[t_idx])
                space = cap - curr
                if space <= 0:
                    continue

                qty = min(space, remaining)
                if qty <= 0:
                    continue

                moves.append({
                    "Material": material,
                    "Description": str(src.get("Description", "")),
                    "FromBin": str(src["Bin"]),
                    "ToBin": str(tgt["Bin"]),
                    "Quantity": float(qty),
                })

                remaining -= qty
                tgt_qty[t_idx] = curr + qty
                if remaining <= 0:
                    break

    return moves


# =========================
# GUI widgets
# =========================

class ColumnMapperDialog(tk.Toplevel):
    def __init__(self, parent, columns, required_keys):
        super().__init__(parent)
        self.title("Map Columns (one-time per file)")
        self.resizable(False, False)
        self.result = {}

        ttk.Label(self, text="Auto-detection failed. Pick the correct columns and click OK.").grid(
            row=0, column=0, columnspan=2, padx=12, pady=(12, 8), sticky="w"
        )

        self.vars = {}
        row = 1
        for key in required_keys:
            ttk.Label(self, text=f"{key.capitalize()} column:").grid(row=row, column=0, padx=12, pady=6, sticky="e")
            v = tk.StringVar(value="")
            cb = ttk.Combobox(self, textvariable=v, values=[""] + list(columns), width=45, state="readonly")
            cb.grid(row=row, column=1, padx=12, pady=6, sticky="w")
            self.vars[key] = v
            row += 1

        btns = ttk.Frame(self)
        btns.grid(row=row, column=0, columnspan=2, padx=12, pady=(10, 12), sticky="e")

        ttk.Button(btns, text="Cancel", command=self._cancel).pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=6)
        ttk.Button(btns, text="OK", command=self._ok).pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=6)

        self.grab_set()
        self.protocol("WM_DELETE_WINDOW", self._cancel)

    def _ok(self):
        self.result = {k: v.get().strip() for k, v in self.vars.items() if v.get().strip() != ""}
        self.destroy()

    def _cancel(self):
        self.result = {}
        self.destroy()


class ScrollFrame(ttk.Frame):
    def __init__(self, parent):
        super().__init__(parent)
        canvas = tk.Canvas(self, highlightthickness=0)
        vsb = ttk.Scrollbar(self, orient="vertical", command=canvas.yview)
        self.inner = ttk.Frame(canvas)

        self.inner.bind("<Configure>", lambda e: canvas.configure(scrollregion=canvas.bbox("all")))
        canvas.create_window((0, 0), window=self.inner, anchor="nw")
        canvas.configure(yscrollcommand=vsb.set)

        canvas.pack(side="left", fill="both", expand=True)
        vsb.pack(side="right", fill="y")

        def _on_mousewheel(event):
            try:
                canvas.yview_scroll(int(-1*(event.delta/120)), "units")
            except Exception:
                pass
        canvas.bind_all("<MouseWheel>", _on_mousewheel)


# =========================
# Main App
# =========================

class ConsolidatorApp:
    def __init__(self, root: tk.Tk):
        self.root = root
        self.root.title("Consolidator – Row Capacity Override")
        self.root.geometry("1200x760")

        self.file_path = tk.StringVar()
        self.threshold = tk.IntVar(value=40)
        self.status = tk.StringVar(value="Ready.")

        # Row capacity dropdowns (no defaults)
        self.row_capacity_vars = {}  # row_id -> StringVar
        self.current_rows_signature = None

        self.text_display = None
        self.row_cap_scroll = None

        self._setup_ui()

    def _setup_ui(self):
        main = ttk.Frame(self.root, padding="10")
        main.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)

        top = ttk.Frame(main)
        top.pack(fill=tk.X)

        file_frame = ttk.LabelFrame(top, text="Input Export (XLSX / HTML / XML)", padding="10")
        file_frame.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.X, expand=True, pady=6)

        ttk.Entry(file_frame, textvariable=self.file_path, width=90).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)
        ttk.Button(file_frame, text="Browse", command=self.browse_file).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)

        controls = ttk.LabelFrame(top, text="Controls", padding="10")
        controls.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, fill=tk.Y, padx=(10,0), pady=6)

        ttk.Label(controls, text="Threshold (bins >= are sources):").pack(anchor="w")
        ttk.Spinbox(controls, from_=1, to=999, increment=1, textvariable=self.threshold, width=8).pack(anchor="w", pady=(0,8))

        ttk.Button(controls, text="Generate Report", command=self.process_file).pack(fill=tk.X, pady=(0,6))
        ttk.Button(controls, text="Save Report", command=self.save_results).pack(fill=tk.X)

        ttk.Label(main, textvariable=self.status).pack(anchor="w", pady=(2,8))

        mid = ttk.Frame(main)
        mid.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)

        # Row capacity panel (left)
        rowcap = ttk.LabelFrame(mid, text="Row Bin Capacity Overrides (required)", padding="10")
        rowcap.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.Y, padx=(0,10))

        ttk.Label(rowcap, text="Set capacity per Row (2–45). No defaults.\nReport won't run until all rows are set.").pack(anchor="w", pady=(0,8))

        self.row_cap_scroll = ScrollFrame(rowcap)
        self.row_cap_scroll.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)

        # Results panel (right)
        box = ttk.LabelFrame(mid, text="Consolidation Moves", padding="10")
        box.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)

        self.text_display = tk.Text(box, wrap=tk.NONE, font=("Consolas", 10))
        vs = ttk.Scrollbar(box, orient=tk.VERTICAL, command=self.text_display.yview)
        hs = ttk.Scrollbar(box, orient=tk.HORIZONTAL, command=self.text_display.xview)
        self.text_display.configure(yscrollcommand=vs.set, xscrollcommand=hs.set)

        self.text_display.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)
        vs.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, fill=tk.Y)
        hs.pack(side=tk.BOTTOM, fill=tk.X)

        ttk.Label(main, text="Tip: If your work laptop blocks EXEs from USB, copy Consolidator.exe to C:\\temp first.").pack(anchor="w", pady=(6,0))

    def browse_file(self):
        fn = filedialog.askopenfilename(
            filetypes=[
                ("Supported", "*.xlsx *.xls *.xml *.htm *.html"),
                ("Excel", "*.xlsx *.xls"),
                ("XML", "*.xml"),
                ("HTML", "*.htm *.html"),
                ("All files", "*.*"),
            ]
        )
        if fn:
            self.file_path.set(fn)
            self.status.set("Selected file: " + fn)
            self._reset_row_capacities()

    def _reset_row_capacities(self):
        self.row_capacity_vars = {}
        self.current_rows_signature = None
        for child in self.row_cap_scroll.inner.winfo_children():
            child.destroy()

    def _interactive_mapper(self, df, keys):
        dlg = ColumnMapperDialog(self.root, list(df.columns), keys)
        self.root.wait_window(dlg)
        return dlg.result

    def _ensure_row_capacity_controls(self, rows):
        signature = ",".join(rows)
        if signature == self.current_rows_signature:
            return

        for child in self.row_cap_scroll.inner.winfo_children():
            child.destroy()

        self.row_capacity_vars = {}
        self.current_rows_signature = signature

        values = [str(i) for i in range(2, 46)]  # 2–45 inclusive

        for row_id in rows:
            fr = ttk.Frame(self.row_cap_scroll.inner)
            fr.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=2)

            ttk.Label(fr, text=f"Row {row_id}:", width=10).pack(side=tk.LEFT)
            v = tk.StringVar(value="")  # no default
            cb = ttk.Combobox(fr, textvariable=v, values=values, width=8, state="readonly")
            cb.pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=6)

            self.row_capacity_vars[row_id] = v

    def _apply_row_capacities(self, df: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:
        rows = sorted([str(r) for r in df["Row"].dropna().unique() if str(r).strip() != ""])
        self._ensure_row_capacity_controls(rows)

        missing = [r for r in rows if self.row_capacity_vars[r].get().strip() == ""]
        if missing:
            messagebox.showerror("Row capacities required", "Set capacity (2–45) for rows:\n" + ", ".join(missing))
            raise MappingError("Row capacity not set for all rows.")

        cap_map = {r: float(self.row_capacity_vars[r].get().strip()) for r in rows}
        df = df.copy()
        df["Capacity"] = df["Row"].astype(str).map(lambda r: cap_map.get(r, 0.0))
        return df

    def process_file(self):
        path = self.file_path.get().strip()
        if not path:
            return messagebox.showerror("Error", "Select an export file first.")

        try:
            self.status.set("Parsing export…")
            df = parse_any_to_standard(path, interactive_mapper=self._interactive_mapper)

            if df.empty:
                self._print("Parsed 0 usable rows.")
                self.status.set("Parsed 0 rows.")
                return

            df = self._apply_row_capacities(df)
            self.status.set(f"Parsed {len(df)} rows. Building moves…")

            threshold = int(self.threshold.get())
            moves = build_moves(df, threshold)

            if not moves:
                self._print(f"No moves found.\nEither bins >= {threshold} are already empty, or there is no space in bins < {threshold} (using your row capacities).")
                self.status.set("No moves found.")
                return

            lines = []
            lines.append(f"INPUT: {path}")
            lines.append(f"THRESHOLD: {threshold} (bins >= threshold are emptied; bins < threshold are targets)")
            lines.append("CAPACITY OVERRIDE: per-row dropdowns (2–45)")
            lines.append(f"MOVES: {len(moves)}\n")
            lines.append(f"{'MATERIAL':<14} | {'FROM':<12} -> {'TO':<12} | {'QTY':>10} | DESCRIPTION")
            lines.append("-" * 110)

            for m in moves:
                lines.append(f"{m['Material']:<14} | {m['FromBin']:<12} -> {m['ToBin']:<12} | {m['Quantity']:>10.2f} | {m['Description']}")

            self._print("\n".join(lines))
            self.status.set(f"Done. {len(moves)} moves.")

        except MappingError:
            self.status.set("Needs row capacities / mapping.")
        except Exception as e:
            self.status.set("Error.")
            messagebox.showerror("Error", f"Failed to process file:\n{e}")

    def _print(self, text: str):
        self.text_display.delete("1.0", tk.END)
        self.text_display.insert(tk.END, text)

    def save_results(self):
        txt = self.text_display.get("1.0", tk.END).strip()
        if not txt:
            return
        out = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(defaultextension=".txt", filetypes=[("Text files", "*.txt"), ("All files", "*.*")])
        if not out:
            return
        try:
            with open(out, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                f.write(txt + "\n")
            messagebox.showinfo("Saved", f"Saved:\n{out}")
        except Exception as e:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", f"Could not save:\n{e}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = tk.Tk()
    ConsolidatorApp(root)
    root.mainloop()
